top: 5628px; left: 1810px; z-index: 256; letter-spacing: 0.27px;">注意人格分析中</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-0" style="width: 47px; height: 204px; line-height: 204px; top: 5628px; left: 3145px; z-index: 257;">,</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-4" style="width: 2481px; height: 204px; line-height: 204px; top: 5628px; left: 3195px; z-index: 258; letter-spacing: 0.4px;">括号内代表该型人格在（压力</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-0" style="width: 52px; height: 204px; line-height: 204px; top: 5628px; left: 5679px; z-index: 259;">\</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-4" style="width: 2289px; height: 204px; line-height: 204px; top: 5628px; left: 5731px; z-index: 260; letter-spacing: 0.29px;">安逸）状况下的延伸人格，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-4" style="width: 3048px; height: 190px; line-height: 190px; top: 5875px; left: 1429px; z-index: 261;">即每一种人格都是三方面的联合体。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-0" style="width: 47px; height: 190px; line-height: 190px; top: 5875px; left: 4477px; z-index: 262; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-4" style="width: 5740px; height: 190px; line-height: 190px; top: 6123px; left: 1810px; z-index: 263; letter-spacing: 0.83px;">第一方面是主宰方面，在日常环境中发挥作用，也就是通常被认定的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-7" style="width: 84px; height: 190px; line-height: 190px; top: 6123px; left: 7554px; z-index: 264;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-4 reader-word-s1-9" style="width: 382px; height: 190px; line-height: 190px; top: 6123px; left: 7640px; z-index: 265; font-size: 190px;">你的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-4" style="width: 380px; height: 190px; line-height: 190px; top: 6371px; left: 1429px; z-index: 266;">类型</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-7" style="width: 84px; height: 190px; line-height: 190px; top: 6371px; left: 1810px; z-index: 267;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-4" style="width: 190px; height: 190px; line-height: 190px; top: 6371px; left: 1893px; z-index: 268;">；</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-0" style="width: 47px; height: 190px; line-height: 190px; top: 6371px; left: 2084px; z-index: 269; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-4" style="width: 5333px; height: 190px; line-height: 190px; top: 6618px; left: 1810px; z-index: 270;">第二方面的性格是当你处于行动状态或受到压力时发挥作用的；</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-0" style="width: 47px; height: 190px; line-height: 190px; top: 6618px; left: 7145px; z-index: 271; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-4" style="width: 4954px; height: 190px; line-height: 190px; top: 6866px; left: 1810px; z-index: 272;">第三方面的性格是在安全状态下即毫无压力时发挥作用的。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-0" style="width: 47px; height: 190px; line-height: 190px; top: 6866px; left: 6764px; z-index: 273; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-4" style="width: 6095px; height: 190px; line-height: 190px; top: 7114px; left: 1810px; z-index: 274;">因此，在评价自身性格时需要参考压力状态下和安全状态下的延伸性格。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-0" style="width: 47px; height: 190px; line-height: 190px; top: 7114px; left: 7907px; z-index: 275; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-0" style="width: 47px; height: 204px; line-height: 204px; top: 7361px; left: 1429px; z-index: 276; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-0" style="width: 47px; height: 204px; line-height: 204px; top: 7361px; left: 1524px; z-index: 277; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-0" style="width: 47px; height: 204px; line-height: 204px; top: 7361px; left: 1619px; z-index: 278; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-0" style="width: 47px; height: 204px; line-height: 204px; top: 7361px; left: 1714px; z-index: 279; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-0" style="width: 47px; height: 204px; line-height: 204px; top: 7361px; left: 1810px; z-index: 280; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-0" style="width: 47px; height: 204px; line-height: 204px; top: 7361px; left: 1905px; z-index: 281; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-11" style="width: 668px; height: 167px; line-height: 167px; top: 7846px; left: 1429px; z-index: 282; letter-spacing: -0.58px;">九型人格</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-12" style="width: 83px; height: 167px; line-height: 167px; top: 7846px; left: 2097px; z-index: 283;">1</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-14" style="width: 501px; height: 167px; line-height: 167px; top: 7846px; left: 2179px; z-index: 284;">号性格</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-8 reader-word-s1-13" style="width: 501px; height: 167px; line-height: 167px; top: 7846px; left: 2681px; z-index: 285; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, cc50ea2ced630b1c59eeb5b80030001, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">———</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-14" style="width: 1501px; height: 167px; line-height: 167px; top: 7846px; left: 3180px; z-index: 286;">完美主义者、管家婆</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-12" style="width: 41px; height: 167px; line-height: 167px; top: 7846px; left: 4679px; z-index: 287; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-16" style="width: 795px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 8317px; left: 1429px; z-index: 288; letter-spacing: 1.23px;">领导特质－</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-20" style="width: 79px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 8317px; left: 2227px; z-index: 289;">1</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-16" style="width: 316px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 8317px; left: 2307px; z-index: 290;">号属</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-22" style="width: 79px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 8317px; left: 2625px; z-index: 291;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-16 reader-word-s1-23" style="width: 476px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 8317px; left: 2705px; z-index: 292; font-weight: 600; color: rgb(255, 0, 0);">管家婆</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-22" style="width: 79px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 8317px; left: 3183px; z-index: 293;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-12" style="width: 41px; height: 167px; line-height: 167px; top: 8309px; left: 3262px; z-index: 294; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-20" style="width: 39px; height: 170px; line-height: 170px; top: 8565px; left: 1429px; z-index: 295; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-20" style="width: 39px; height: 170px; line-height: 170px; top: 8565px; left: 1509px; z-index: 296; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-20" style="width: 39px; height: 170px; line-height: 170px; top: 8565px; left: 1589px; z-index: 297; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-16" style="width: 6369px; height: 170px; line-height: 170px; top: 8565px; left: 1669px; z-index: 298; letter-spacing: 1.09px;">很有原则，关注细节、小地方和丑陋的东西。易挑毛病、看负面的东西；完美主义、教条、</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-16" style="width: 478px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 8812px; left: 1429px; z-index: 299; letter-spacing: 1.8px;">规矩！</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-12" style="width: 41px; height: 167px; line-height: 167px; top: 8804px; left: 1907px; z-index: 300; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-20" style="width: 79px; height: 170px; line-height: 170px; top: 9060px; left: 1429px; z-index: 301;">1</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-16" style="width: 2866px; height: 170px; line-height: 170px; top: 9060px; left: 1509px; z-index: 302; letter-spacing: 1.16px;">号性格才力属正将，公平、公正、规范！</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-12" style="width: 41px; height: 180px; line-height: 180px; top: 9052px; left: 4378px; z-index: 303; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-9 reader-word-s1-26" style="width: 638px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 9308px; left: 1429px; z-index: 304; letter-spacing: 1.79px;">一、困境</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-12" style="width: 41px; height: 167px; line-height: 167px; top: 9299px; left: 2067px; z-index: 305; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-24" style="width: 1744px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 9555px; left: 1747px; z-index: 306; letter-spacing: 0.49px;">完美主义者们勤劳工作、</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-27" style="width: 792px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 9555px; left: 3466px; z-index: 307;">有正义感、</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-27" style="width: 792px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 9555px; left: 4236px; z-index: 308;">完全独立，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-28" style="width: 3014px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 9555px; left: 5003px; z-index: 309;">并且坚信朴素的思想和善良必将战胜人性的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-24" style="width: 5497px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 9803px; left: 1429px; z-index: 310; letter-spacing: -1.01px;">阴暗面。他们相信生活是艰难的，安逸是用汗水换取的，德行是对自己的奖赏，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-28" style="width: 1110px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 9803px; left: 6907px; z-index: 311;">而快乐只有在其</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-24" style="width: 1902px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 10051px; left: 1429px; z-index: 312; letter-spacing: 0.44px;">他事情都完成后才能获得。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-12" style="width: 41px; height: 167px; line-height: 167px; top: 10043px; left: 3334px; z-index: 313; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-29" style="width: 6243px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 10299px; left: 1773px; z-index: 314;">一个完美主义者的注意力被完全集中在应该做和必须做的事情上。他们的大脑中已经没有</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-24" style="width: 3648px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 10546px; left: 1429px; z-index: 315; letter-spacing: 0.52px;">空间去关注他们自身的希望。因此，他们总是不满。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-12" style="width: 41px; height: 167px; line-height: 167px; top: 10538px; left: 5081px; z-index: 316; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-29" style="width: 6243px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 10794px; left: 1773px; z-index: 317;">完美主义者的世界观来自于这样一个假想：世界上的每一个问题最终都有一个正确的解决</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-28" style="width: 5870px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 11042px; left: 1429px; z-index: 318;">办法。他们把这种惟一的正确性视作追求的目标，不管有没有其他更吸引人的方式。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-12" style="width: 41px; height: 167px; line-height: 167px; top: 11033px; left: 7303px; z-index: 319; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-29" style="width: 6243px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 11289px; left: 1773px; z-index: 320;">对于有些完美主义者而言，为了平衡矛盾，让住在房间里的内心批评家和藏在地下室里不</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-24" style="width: 3806px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 11537px; left: 1429px; z-index: 321; letter-spacing: 0.5px;">被察觉的情感能够和睦相处，他们会选择在地板上安装</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-30" style="width: 70px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 11537px; left: 5239px; z-index: 322;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-23 reader-word-s1-24" style="width: 476px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 11537px; left: 5308px; z-index: 323; letter-spacing: 0.82px;">活动门</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-30" style="width: 70px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 11537px; left: 5784px; z-index: 324;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-24" style="width: 158px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 11537px; left: 5854px; z-index: 325;">。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-12" style="width: 41px; height: 167px; line-height: 167px; top: 11529px; left: 6015px; z-index: 326; font-family: simsun;"></p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-26" style="width: 1273px; height: 158px; line-height: 158px; top: 11784px; left: 1429px; z-index: 327; letter-spacing: 1.17px;">二、主要性格特征</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s1-12" style="width: 41px; height: 167px; line-height: 167px; top: 11776px; left: 2703px;                 <div class="ie-fix"><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 1186px;left: 1773px;z-index: 2;;;;;;null;">1</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-5" style="width: 2852px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 1186px;left: 1853px;z-index: 3;;;;;;false;">号对于那些破坏规则的人可能非常愤怒。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 1178px;left: 4710px;z-index: 4;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 1434px;left: 1773px;z-index: 5;;;;;;null;">1</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-7" style="width: 5393px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 1434px;left: 1853px;z-index: 6;;;;;;false;">号性格者说，他人的批评是一种极大的痛苦，因为他们已经饱受自责的折磨。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 1425px;left: 7251px;z-index: 7;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 3161px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1681px;left: 1773px;z-index: 8;;;;;;false;">一面是沉睡的欲望，另一面是对正确的要求，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1681px;left: 4925px;z-index: 9;;;;;;null;">1</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-8" style="width: 3012px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1681px;left: 5005px;z-index: 10;;;;;;false;">号性格者的两个方面往往会让他们陷入两难</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 474px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1929px;left: 1429px;z-index: 11;;;;;;false;">境界。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 1270px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1929px;left: 1852px;z-index: 12;letter-spacing: 0.7000000000000001px;;;;;;false;">如果选择正确的，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-9" style="width: 3490px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1929px;left: 3070px;z-index: 13;;;;;;false;">他们可能会因为没有等到自己真正想要的而生气；</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 1588px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1929px;left: 6509px;z-index: 14;letter-spacing: 0.73px;;;;;;false;">如果选择自己想要的，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-9" style="width: 2062px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2177px;left: 1429px;z-index: 15;;;;;;false;">他们又会担心因此而犯错误。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2168px;left: 3492px;z-index: 16;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 6324px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2424px;left: 1773px;z-index: 17;;;;;;false;">他们努力打造最优秀的爱情。他们会重新对自己的伴侣进行包装，忘记对方性格中的缺点，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-10" style="width: 3172px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 1429px;z-index: 18;;;;;;false;">让自己忘记任何人都是一个优缺点的混合体。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-9" style="width: 2062px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 4563px;z-index: 19;;;;;;false;">一旦他们发现了某人的优点，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-11" style="width: 1426px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 6589px;z-index: 20;;;;;;false;">完美主义者就会坚信</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-12" style="width: 2854px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2920px;left: 1429px;z-index: 21;;;;;;false;">自己能够把对方身上不完美的地主去掉。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2911px;left: 4287px;z-index: 22;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-13" style="width: 6243px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3167px;left: 1773px;z-index: 23;;;;;;false;">如果他们能够找到一个能干的领导者，他们很愿意把决策权交给对方。不过也正是因为他</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-10" style="width: 4758px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3415px;left: 1429px;z-index: 24;;;;;;false;">们天性追求正确，让他们对于领导者不公平或错误的表现非常敏感。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3407px;left: 6192px;z-index: 25;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 3662px;left: 1773px;z-index: 26;;;;;;null;">1</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 6162px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 3662px;left: 1853px;z-index: 27;;;;;;false;">号性格者的心中时刻竖立着完美的标杆，在与自己较劲儿的同时，还和他人进行比较。这</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-9" style="width: 1586px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3910px;left: 1429px;z-index: 28;;;;;;false;">种内心的比较，往往是</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3910px;left: 3016px;z-index: 29;;;;;;null;">1</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 4922px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3910px;left: 3096px;z-index: 30;letter-spacing: 0.65px;;;;;;false;">号性格者在日常生活中不经意做出的，却是他们感到痛苦的一个主要原</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 316px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4158px;left: 1429px;z-index: 31;;;;;;false;">因。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4150px;left: 1747px;z-index: 32;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-13" style="width: 6243px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 1773px;z-index: 33;;;;;;false;">真正的完美，来自于正面因素和负面因素的时时平衡。事实上，完美的条件并不是一成不</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 2974px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 1429px;z-index: 34;letter-spacing: -1.53px;;;;;;false;">变的，而是根据不同情况变化的。如果信奉</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-14" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 4407px;z-index: 35;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-15" style="width: 794px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 4477px;z-index: 36;;;;;;false;">唯一正确性</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-14" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 5272px;z-index: 37;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-16" style="width: 2380px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 5342px;z-index: 38;;;;;;false;">的完美主义者能够意识到这一点，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 316px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 7703px;z-index: 39;;;;;;false;">他们</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-17" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4901px;left: 1429px;z-index: 40;;;;;;false;">就进入了更高的思想境界。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4893px;left: 3334px;z-index: 41;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 6239px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 1773px;z-index: 42;letter-spacing: 1.8199999999999998px;;;;;;false;">如果他们能够让所有的冲动和欲望暴露出来，他们就能获得一种平静的心态。在这种心态</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 4880px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5396px;left: 1429px;z-index: 43;letter-spacing: -0.64px;;;;;;false;">中，他们每时每刻都处于平衡之中。所有正面和负面的感觉互相交织，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 1428px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5396px;left: 6290px;z-index: 44;letter-spacing: 0.61px;;;;;;false;">在身体内自由流动，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 316px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5396px;left: 7700px;z-index: 45;;;;;;false;">无需</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-18" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5644px;left: 1429px;z-index: 46;;;;;;false;">躲避理性的自我。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5636px;left: 2700px;z-index: 47;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-20" style="width: 478px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5892px;left: 1429px;z-index: 48;letter-spacing: 1.7999999999999998px;;;;;;false;">三、对</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-21" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5892px;left: 1909px;z-index: 49;;;;;;null;">1</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-20" style="width: 955px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5892px;left: 1987px;z-index: 50;letter-spacing: 1.31px;;;;;;false;">号有利的做法</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5884px;left: 2943px;z-index: 51;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 6139px;left: 1429px;z-index: 52;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 6139px;left: 1509px;z-index: 53;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 6139px;left: 1589px;z-index: 54;;;;;;null;">1</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-16" style="width: 6348px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 6139px;left: 1669px;z-index: 55;;;;;;false;">、不要强迫自己做事：不要把自己的工作安排得满满当当，以至于没有时间思考真正重要的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 474px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6387px;left: 1429px;z-index: 56;;;;;;false;">需求。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6379px;left: 1905px;z-index: 57;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 6635px;left: 1512px;z-index: 58;;;;;;null;">2</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-18" style="width: 4123px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 6635px;left: 1592px;z-index: 59;;;;;;false;">、需要对内心的严格标准进行修改。需要对规则提出质疑。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 6626px;left: 5719px;z-index: 60;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 6882px;left: 1512px;z-index: 61;;;;;;null;">3</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-5" style="width: 2852px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 6882px;left: 1592px;z-index: 62;;;;;;false;">、不要把自己的洞察变成对自己的攻击。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-14" style="width: 70px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 6882px;left: 4449px;z-index: 63;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-9" style="width: 2538px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 6882px;left: 4519px;z-index: 64;;;;;;false;">我怎么会连自己的错误都发现不了？</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-14" style="width: 70px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 6882px;left: 7061px;z-index: 65;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 6874px;left: 7131px;z-index: 66;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7130px;left: 1512px;z-index: 67;;;;;;null;">4</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 4085px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7130px;left: 1592px;z-index: 68;letter-spacing: -0.96px;;;;;;false;">、到现实中去找答案。如果觉得其他人在对自己品头论足，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-22" style="width: 1904px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7130px;left: 5659px;z-index: 69;;;;;;false;">那就直接找他们问问清楚。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 474px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7130px;left: 7544px;z-index: 70;;;;;;false;">如果感</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-7" style="width: 4441px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7378px;left: 1429px;z-index: 71;;;;;;false;">到自己的担忧在加剧，就去寻找事实信息来消除不必要的焦虑。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7370px;left: 5874px;z-index: 72;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7626px;left: 1512px;z-index: 73;;;;;;null;">5</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 474px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7626px;left: 1592px;z-index: 74;;;;;;false;">、知道</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-14" style="width: 70px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7626px;left: 2069px;z-index: 75;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-11" style="width: 792px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7626px;left: 2137px;z-index: 76;;;;;;false;">惟一正确性</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-14" style="width: 70px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7626px;left: 2930px;z-index: 77;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-9" style="width: 3966px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7626px;left: 3002px;z-index: 78;;;;;;false;">的思想会限制妥协的机会，或者与其他观点交流的机会。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 7617px;left: 6973px;z-index: 79;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7873px;left: 1512px;z-index: 80;;;;;;null;">6</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-8" style="width: 3012px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7873px;left: 1592px;z-index: 81;;;;;;false;">、关注其他人思想观念中的价值和一贯性。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 7865px;left: 4609px;z-index: 82;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8121px;left: 1512px;z-index: 83;;;;;;null;">7</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-11" style="width: 2060px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8121px;left: 1592px;z-index: 84;;;;;;false;">、学会寻找快乐和接受快乐。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 8113px;left: 3656px;z-index: 85;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8368px;left: 1512px;z-index: 86;;;;;;null;">8</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 790px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8368px;left: 1592px;z-index: 87;;;;;;false;">、学会区分</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-14" style="width: 70px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8368px;left: 2385px;z-index: 88;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 316px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8368px;left: 2455px;z-index: 89;;;;;;false;">应该</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-14" style="width: 70px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8368px;left: 2772px;z-index: 90;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-15" style="width: 476px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8368px;left: 2842px;z-index: 91;;;;;;false;">完成和</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-14" style="width: 70px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8368px;left: 3321px;z-index: 92;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 316px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8368px;left: 3391px;z-index: 93;;;;;;false;">想要</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-14" style="width: 70px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8368px;left: 3707px;z-index: 94;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-18" style="width: 1268px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8368px;left: 3778px;z-index: 95;;;;;;false;">完成之间的差别。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 8360px;left: 5049px;z-index: 96;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8616px;left: 1512px;z-index: 97;;;;;;null;">9</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-8" style="width: 4757px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8616px;left: 1592px;z-index: 98;;;;;;false;">、关注你对他人的怒火，很可能他人的所做所为正是你内心渴望的。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 8608px;left: 6354px;z-index: 99;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-23" style="width: 159px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8864px;left: 1512px;z-index: 100;;;;;;false;">10</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 6345px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8864px;left: 1672px;z-index: 101;letter-spacing: 0.5px;;;;;;false;">、注意未被察觉的生气现象：比如内心很生气，表面还故意摆出笑脸；言语很礼貌，但声音</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-10" style="width: 2696px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9111px;left: 1429px;z-index: 102;;;;;;false;">很尖刻；或者面带笑容，但动作僵硬。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9103px;left: 4128px;z-index: 103;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 153px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 9359px;left: 1512px;z-index: 104;letter-spacing: -4.5px;;;;;;false;">11</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-11" style="width: 2060px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 9359px;left: 1667px;z-index: 105;;;;;;false;">、学会让阴影情绪发泄出来。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 9351px;left: 3730px;z-index: 106;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-23" style="width: 159px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 9607px;left: 1512px;z-index: 107;;;;;;false;">12</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 4442px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 9607px;left: 1672px;z-index: 108;letter-spacing: 0.55px;;;;;;false;">、运用想象力来化解怒气。想象最糟糕的情况，直到怒气消失。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 9598px;left: 6118px;z-index: 109;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-20" style="width: 318px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9855px;left: 1512px;z-index: 110;letter-spacing: 1.79px;;;;;;false;">四、</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-21" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9855px;left: 1832px;z-index: 111;;;;;;null;">1</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-20" style="width: 1271px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9855px;left: 1912px;z-index: 112;letter-spacing: 0.9299999999999999px;;;;;;false;">号需要注意的做法</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9847px;left: 3185px;z-index: 113;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10102px;left: 1512px;z-index: 114;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10102px;left: 1592px;z-index: 115;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10102px;left: 1672px;z-index: 116;;;;;;null;">1</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-17" style="width: 3646px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10102px;left: 1752px;z-index: 117;;;;;;false;">、感到有两个自己存在，一个很快乐，一个很严厉。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 10094px;left: 5401px;z-index: 118;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10350px;left: 1512px;z-index: 119;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10350px;left: 1592px;z-index: 120;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10350px;left: 1672px;z-index: 121;;;;;;null;">2</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-24" style="width: 1900px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10350px;left: 1752px;z-index: 122;;;;;;false;">、对个人的希望毫无察觉。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 10342px;left: 3656px;z-index: 123;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10598px;left: 1512px;z-index: 124;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10598px;left: 1592px;z-index: 125;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10598px;left: 1672px;z-index: 126;;;;;;null;">3</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-25" style="width: 3011px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10598px;left: 1752px;z-index: 127;;;;;;false;">、因为察觉到自己内心的怒火而感到焦虑，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-14" style="width: 70px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10598px;left: 4767px;z-index: 128;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-22" style="width: 1904px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10598px;left: 4835px;z-index: 129;;;;;;false;">我设法不要对别人发脾气。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-14" style="width: 70px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10598px;left: 6741px;z-index: 130;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 10590px;left: 6813px;z-index: 131;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10845px;left: 1512px;z-index: 132;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10845px;left: 1672px;z-index: 134;;;;;;null;">4</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-25" style="width: 3011px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10845px;left: 1752px;z-index: 135;;;;;;false;">、把时间都占满了，没有给快乐留下时间。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 10837px;left: 4767px;z-index: 136;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11093px;left: 1512px;z-index: 137;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11093px;left: 1592px;z-index: 138;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11093px;left: 1672px;z-index: 139;;;;;;null;">5</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 4121px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11093px;left: 1752px;z-index: 140;letter-spacing: 0.39px;;;;;;false;">、犹豫不决。把简单的问题复杂化，不愿做出最后的承诺。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 11085px;left: 5877px;z-index: 141;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11341px;left: 1512px;z-index: 142;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11341px;left: 1592px;z-index: 143;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11341px;left: 1672px;z-index: 144;;;;;;null;">6</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-12" style="width: 5551px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11341px;left: 1752px;z-index: 145;;;;;;false;">、被压抑的需求找不到表达途径，导致自身压力不断增大，不满情绪随之增强。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 11332px;left: 7307px;z-index: 146;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11588px;left: 1512px;z-index: 147;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11588px;left: 1592px;z-index: 148;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11588px;left: 1672px;z-index: 149;;;;;;null;">7</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-24" style="width: 1900px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11588px;left: 1752px;z-index: 150;;;;;;false;">、需要从环境中找到错误。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-6" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 11580px;left: 3656px;z-index: 151;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11836px;left: 1512px;z-index: 152;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11836px;left: 1592px;z-index: 153;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-2" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11836px;left: 1672px;z-index: 154;;;;;;null;">8</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 5968px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11836px;left: 1752px;z-index: 155;letter-spacing: -1px;;;;;;false;">、注意力僵硬。把所有的注意力都放在生活中需要改进的地方，对其他方面毫不关心。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s2-4" style="width: 316px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11836px;left: 7702px;z-index: 156;;;;;;false;">把内

                <div class="ie-fix"><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-1" style="width: 316px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1186px;left: 1587px;z-index: 2;;;;;;false;">对于</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-5" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1186px;left: 1903px;z-index: 3;;;;;;null;">2</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-1" style="width: 6034px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1186px;left: 1983px;z-index: 4;letter-spacing: 0.66px;;;;;;false;">号性格来说，他们给予对方的东西，一定也是他们希望得到的回报。如果他们贡献了雨</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-1" style="width: 316px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1434px;left: 1429px;z-index: 5;;;;;;false;">伞，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-6" style="width: 2220px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1434px;left: 1720px;z-index: 6;;;;;;false;">他们一定也希望自己不要淋雨。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-7" style="width: 2062px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1434px;left: 3918px;z-index: 7;;;;;;false;">如果他们记住了别人的生日，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-7" style="width: 2062px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1434px;left: 5955px;z-index: 8;;;;;;false;">他们一定也希望自己的生日被</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-8" style="width: 792px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1681px;left: 1429px;z-index: 9;;;;;;false;">别人记住。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-9" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 1673px;left: 2223px;z-index: 10;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-5" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 1929px;left: 1773px;z-index: 11;;;;;;null;">2</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-1" style="width: 6162px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 1929px;left: 1853px;z-index: 12;;;;;;false;">号性格者的哲学是：任何人都是可以征服的。只要找到正确的方式，并加以适当的特别关</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-1" style="width: 316px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2177px;left: 1429px;z-index: 13;;;;;;false;">注。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-7" style="width: 634px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2177px;left: 1720px;z-index: 14;;;;;;false;">事实上，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-7" style="width: 634px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2177px;left: 2329px;z-index: 15;;;;;;false;">大部分的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-5" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2177px;left: 2964px;z-index: 16;;;;;;null;">2</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-1" style="width: 2541px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2177px;left: 3044px;z-index: 17;letter-spacing: 0.72px;;;;;;false;">号性格者能够准确把握他人的感情，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-7" style="width: 2538px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2177px;left: 5561px;z-index: 18;;;;;;false;">从而选择正确的方式来与对方相处。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-9" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2168px;left: 8023px;z-index: 19;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-5" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 2424px;left: 1773px;z-index: 20;;;;;;null;">2</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-1" style="width: 6162px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 2424px;left: 1853px;z-index: 21;;;;;;false;">号性格者是三角关系的常客。他们总是被那些具有某种特质，能够有助于他们个人发展的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-11" style="width: 5711px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 1429px;z-index: 22;;;;;;false;">人所吸引。他们通过帮助别人来帮助自己，所以他们并在乎对象是一个还是多个。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s4-9" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2664px;left: 7145px;z-index: 23;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;">

</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-10" style="width: 1744px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3611px;left: 1747px;z-index: 26;;;;;;false;">看重自己的表现和成就。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3603px;left: 3494px;z-index: 27;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-11" style="width: 792px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3859px;left: 1747px;z-index: 28;;;;;;false;">讲究效率。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3850px;left: 2541px;z-index: 29;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-7" style="width: 1584px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4106px;left: 1747px;z-index: 30;letter-spacing: 0.36px;;;;;;false;">喜欢竞争，避免失败。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4098px;left: 3334px;z-index: 31;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-10" style="width: 3330px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4354px;left: 1747px;z-index: 32;;;;;;false;">相信爱情来自你能提供什么，而不在于你是谁。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4346px;left: 5081px;z-index: 33;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-12" style="width: 3488px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4602px;left: 1747px;z-index: 34;;;;;;false;">只关注事物积极的方面，不理会消极负面的信息。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4594px;left: 5239px;z-index: 35;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-13" style="width: 3966px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4850px;left: 1747px;z-index: 36;;;;;;false;">难以了结个人的感觉。在工作的时候把情感放在了一边。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4842px;left: 5715px;z-index: 37;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-14" style="width: 4282px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5097px;left: 1747px;z-index: 38;;;;;;false;">为争取认可而打造有利性形象。公众形象属于社会高层人物。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5089px;left: 6034px;z-index: 39;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-15" style="width: 2854px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5345px;left: 1747px;z-index: 40;;;;;;false;">在真正自我和工作角色之间会产生困惑。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5337px;left: 4605px;z-index: 41;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-9" style="width: 4761px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5593px;left: 1747px;z-index: 42;;;;;;false;">通过集合思维的方式集中注意力，通过多条渠道来寻找问题的答案。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5584px;left: 6510px;z-index: 43;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-15" style="width: 4440px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5840px;left: 1747px;z-index: 44;;;;;;false;">能够下意识地调整自我形象，以为调整的形象就是个人的真我。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5832px;left: 6192px;z-index: 45;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-12" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6088px;left: 1429px;z-index: 46;;;;;;false;">三、适合的环境：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6080px;left: 2700px;z-index: 47;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-8" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 6336px;left: 1747px;z-index: 48;;;;;;null;">3</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-16" style="width: 6185px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 6336px;left: 1827px;z-index: 49;;;;;;false;">号性格者适合的环境包括那些通过常年打拼，逐步扩大规模的企业。他们可以成为出色的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-7" style="width: 474px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6583px;left: 1429px;z-index: 50;;;;;;false;">经理、</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-11" style="width: 792px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6583px;left: 1865px;z-index: 51;;;;;;false;">销售人员、</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-11" style="width: 792px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6583px;left: 2621px;z-index: 52;;;;;;false;">传媒人士、</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-17" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6583px;left: 3377px;z-index: 53;;;;;;false;">广告业者或者形象工作者。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-15" style="width: 2854px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6583px;left: 5243px;z-index: 54;;;;;;false;">还适合从事那些把想法付诸实施的工作，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-13" style="width: 2062px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6831px;left: 1429px;z-index: 55;;;;;;false;">比如包装、宣传、市场推广。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6823px;left: 3492px;z-index: 56;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-8" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7079px;left: 1747px;z-index: 57;;;;;;null;">3</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-16" style="width: 6185px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7079px;left: 1827px;z-index: 58;;;;;;false;">号性格者会成为他们所属环境中的典型：他们可以是最激进的左翼分子，也可以是最保守</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-18" style="width: 950px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7326px;left: 1429px;z-index: 59;;;;;;false;">的右翼分子。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-14" style="width: 3806px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7326px;left: 2343px;z-index: 60;;;;;;false;">他们总是被那些能够让他们具有成就感的环境所吸引。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-17" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7326px;left: 6113px;z-index: 61;;;;;;false;">他们喜欢具有发展空间的高</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-7" style="width: 632px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7574px;left: 1429px;z-index: 62;;;;;;false;">层职位，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-13" style="width: 1586px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7574px;left: 2038px;z-index: 63;;;;;;false;">比如企业的高层领导。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-19" style="width: 1428px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7574px;left: 3600px;z-index: 64;;;;;;false;">如果他们是政治家，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-7" style="width: 3017px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7574px;left: 5003px;z-index: 65;letter-spacing: 0.7000000000000001px;;;;;;false;">他们会通过媒体形象和个人风格来争取更多</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-7" style="width: 474px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7822px;left: 1429px;z-index: 66;;;;;;false;">选票。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7814px;left: 1905px;z-index: 67;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-11" style="width: 1426px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8069px;left: 1429px;z-index: 68;;;;;;false;">四、不适合的环境：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8061px;left: 2858px;z-index: 69;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-8" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8317px;left: 1747px;z-index: 70;;;;;;null;">3</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-16" style="width: 6185px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8317px;left: 1827px;z-index: 71;;;;;;false;">号性格者不喜欢那些没有发展前途的工作，那些不能给他们带来声望的工作，那些与他们</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-20" style="width: 6029px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8565px;left: 1429px;z-index: 72;;;;;;false;">的社会形象不相符的工作，以及那些需要通过不断反省和尝试才能完成的创造性工作。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-8" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8565px;left: 7461px;z-index: 73;;;;;;null;">3</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-7" style="width: 474px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8565px;left: 7541px;z-index: 74;;;;;;false;">号性格</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-12" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8812px;left: 1429px;z-index: 75;;;;;;false;">者更适合当记者，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-13" style="width: 1110px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8812px;left: 2672px;z-index: 76;;;;;;false;">而不是小说家；</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-19" style="width: 1428px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8812px;left: 3758px;z-index: 77;;;;;;false;">更适合做杂志美编，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-15" style="width: 2854px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8812px;left: 5163px;z-index: 78;;;;;;false;">而不是那些要花上好几个月才能完成一件</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-11" style="width: 1426px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9060px;left: 1429px;z-index: 79;;;;;;false;">作品的严肃艺术家。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9052px;left: 2858px;z-index: 80;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-7" style="width: 474px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9308px;left: 1429px;z-index: 81;;;;;;false;">五、对</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-8" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9308px;left: 1903px;z-index: 82;;;;;;null;">3</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-13" style="width: 1586px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9308px;left: 1983px;z-index: 83;;;;;;false;">号性格者有利的做法：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9299px;left: 3572px;z-index: 84;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-11" style="width: 792px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9555px;left: 1747px;z-index: 85;;;;;;false;">学会停止。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-13" style="width: 2538px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9555px;left: 2501px;z-index: 86;;;;;;false;">给自己的情感和真实思想留下时间。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-7" style="width: 3012px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9555px;left: 5003px;z-index: 87;letter-spacing: 0.44999999999999996px;;;;;;false;">是什么在驱使自己不停地工作？找到这种担</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-7" style="width: 1108px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9803px;left: 1429px;z-index: 88;letter-spacing: 0.27px;;;;;;false;">心并直接面对。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9795px;left: 2539px;z-index: 89;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-13" style="width: 5870px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10051px;left: 1747px;z-index: 90;;;;;;false;">不要让自己的行动变成机械化反应。意识到自己成了生产机器，而情感被全部搁置。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10043px;left: 7621px;z-index: 91;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-12" style="width: 3488px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10299px;left: 1747px;z-index: 92;;;;;;false;">不要让对个人成功的幻想取代了自己的真实能力。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10290px;left: 5239px;z-index: 93;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-18" style="width: 950px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10546px;left: 1747px;z-index: 94;;;;;;false;">遇到困难时，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-13" style="width: 2538px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10546px;left: 2646px;z-index: 95;;;;;;false;">不要通过寻找新的工作来逃避困难，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-12" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10546px;left: 5135px;z-index: 96;;;;;;false;">也不要无视失败，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-7" style="width: 1746px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10546px;left: 6352px;z-index: 97;letter-spacing: 0.65px;;;;;;false;">或者抱怨批评自己的人。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10538px;left: 8023px;z-index: 98;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-7" style="width: 2696px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10794px;left: 1747px;z-index: 99;letter-spacing: 0.51px;;;;;;false;">意识到自己常常会把情感的快乐延迟。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-21" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10794px;left: 4447px;z-index: 100;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-7" style="width: 2856px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10794px;left: 4515px;z-index: 101;letter-spacing: 0.5800000000000001px;;;;;;false;">我完成了下一个推销任务后，就会快乐。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-21" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10794px;left: 7375px;z-index: 102;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10786px;left: 7446px;z-index: 103;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-14" style="width: 4282px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11042px;left: 1747px;z-index: 104;;;;;;false;">认识到真正自我与公众形象的差异。学会从形象中抽离出来。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11033px;left: 6034px;z-index: 105;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-12" style="width: 2378px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11289px;left: 1747px;z-index: 106;;;;;;false;">注意自己的欺骗倾向，喜欢表演。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-21" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11289px;left: 4128px;z-index: 107;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-9" style="width: 3808px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11289px;left: 4197px;z-index: 108;;;;;;false;">没有人会发现面具背后的我；他们只会看到我的所作所</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-7" style="width: 316px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11537px;left: 1429px;z-index: 109;;;;;;false;">为。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-21" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11537px;left: 1745px;z-index: 110;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11529px;left: 1817px;z-index: 111;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-20" style="width: 5076px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11784px;left: 1747px;z-index: 112;;;;;;false;">不要把自己看作离不开的关键人物，把周围的人都看作没有能力的懒汉。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s5-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11776px;left: 6828px;z-index: 113;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p></div></div></div>

</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-9" style="width: 2854px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1681px;left: 1747px;z-index: 8;;;;;;false;">学会通过身体的感觉来发现自己的感觉。</p><p </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-16" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 1747px;z-index: 37;;;;;;false;">对感觉感到困惑。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-4" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 3018px;z-index: 38;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-17" style="width: 1270px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 3086px;z-index: 39;;;;;;false;">我的感觉正确吗？</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-4" style="width: 142px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 4357px;z-index: 40;letter-spacing: 2.07px;;;;;;false;">”“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-17" style="width: 1270px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 4498px;z-index: 41;;;;;;false;">哪个感觉是真的？</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-14" style="width: 39px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 5769px;z-index: 42;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-4" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 5849px;z-index: 43;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3654px;left: 5919px;z-index: 44;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-18" style="width: 6030px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3910px;left: 1747px;z-index: 45;;;;;;false;">在过渡活跃的幻想中生活。在方法根本行不通，或者出现负面效应时，依然幻想成功。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3902px;left: 7781px;z-index: 46;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-9" style="width: 4440px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4158px;left: 1747px;z-index: 47;;;;;;false;">为自己打造虚幻的形象，并且相信这些特质是自己天生具有的。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4150px;left: 6192px;z-index: 48;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-0" style="width: 6269px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 1747px;z-index: 49;letter-spacing: -1.32px;;;;;;false;">急于求成，用工作取代情感需求，并感觉良好。在心理治疗的成果还没有显现时，就想要退</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-0" style="width: 316px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 1429px;z-index: 50;;;;;;false;">出。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4645px;left: 1747px;z-index: 51;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-19" style="width: 1584px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4901px;left: 1747px;z-index: 52;;;;;;false;">需要获得成功的证明。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4893px;left: 3334px;z-index: 53;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-0" style="width: 1426px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 1747px;z-index: 54;letter-spacing: 0.41000000000000003px;;;;;;false;">在讨论个人问题时，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-0" style="width: 2380px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 3148px;z-index: 55;letter-spacing: 0.5800000000000001px;;;;;;false;">总是习惯性地避免讨论自身感觉。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-16" style="width: 2378px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 5506px;z-index: 56;;;;;;false;">觉得个人的问题说一说就能解决，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-0" style="width: 158px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 7859px;z-index: 57;;;;;;null;">无</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-12" style="width: 950px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5396px;left: 1429px;z-index: 58;;;;;;false;">须情感体会。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5388px;left: 2381px;z-index: 59;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-20" style="width: 6345px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5644px;left: 1747px;z-index: 60;;;;;;false;">在接受心理治疗时，倾向于选择十分能干而吸引人的心理医师。看重的是心理医师的价值，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-15" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5892px;left: 1429px;z-index: 61;;;;;;false;">而不是去发现自己的价值。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5884px;left: 3334px;z-index: 62;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-21" style="width: 3330px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6139px;left: 1747px;z-index: 63;;;;;;false;">在冥想的过程中，担心真正的自我根本不存在。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6131px;left: 5081px;z-index: 64;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-22" style="width: 3012px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6387px;left: 1747px;z-index: 65;;;;;;false;">在遭遇他人的批评时，感觉自己像个圣人。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-4" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6387px;left: 4763px;z-index: 66;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-18" style="width: 3173px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6387px;left: 4833px;z-index: 67;;;;;;false;">我做出了那么大的贡献，我根本不用理会那些</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-0" style="width: 474px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6635px;left: 1429px;z-index: 68;;;;;;false;">批评。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-4" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6635px;left: 1903px;z-index: 69;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6626px;left: 1975px;z-index: 70;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 6878px;left: 1429px;z-index: 71;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-0" style="width: 632px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7130px;left: 1429px;z-index: 72;;;;;;false;">九型人格</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-14" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7130px;left: 2061px;z-index: 73;;;;;;null;">4</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-11" style="width: 1110px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7130px;left: 2141px;z-index: 74;;;;;;false;">号型领导特质：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7122px;left: 3254px;z-index: 75;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-14" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7378px;left: 1429px;z-index: 76;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-14" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7378px;left: 1508px;z-index: 77;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-14" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7378px;left: 1588px;z-index: 78;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-14" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7378px;left: 1668px;z-index: 79;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-14" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7378px;left: 1746px;z-index: 80;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-15" style="width: 3646px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7378px;left: 1827px;z-index: 81;;;;;;false;">感觉性、飘逸、喜玩失踪、戏剧人生的感觉、特浪漫</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 7370px;left: 5477px;z-index: 82;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-25" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7626px;left: 1429px;z-index: 83;;;;;;null;">4</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-28" style="width: 3024px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7626px;left: 1509px;z-index: 84;;;;;;false;">号性格属灵将、很容易感受到对方的感觉。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-29" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 7617px;left: 4536px;z-index: 85;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-27" style="width: 638px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7873px;left: 1429px;z-index: 86;letter-spacing: 1.79px;;;;;;false;">一、困境</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7865px;left: 2067px;z-index: 87;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-14" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8121px;left: 1429px;z-index: 88;;;;;;null;">4</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-21" style="width: 6503px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8121px;left: 1509px;z-index: 89;;;;;;false;">号性格者的内心世界就和文学作品中的悲情浪漫者一样，这种人尽管获得了社会的承认和物质</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-0" style="width: 6589px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8368px;left: 1429px;z-index: 90;letter-spacing: -1.18px;;;;;;false;">上的成功，也依然无法开怀。他们渴望得到的是失去的爱、遥远的爱、未来的爱，他们认为只有</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-19" style="width: 1584px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8616px;left: 1429px;z-index: 91;;;;;;false;">这样爱才能带来幸福。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8608px;left: 3016px;z-index: 92;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-14" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8864px;left: 1512px;z-index: 93;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-14" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8864px;left: 1592px;z-index: 94;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-14" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8864px;left: 1672px;z-index: 95;;;;;;null;">4</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-0" style="width: 474px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8864px;left: 1752px;z-index: 96;;;;;;false;">号做出</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-14" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8864px;left: 2227px;z-index: 97;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-3" style="width: 5711px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8864px;left: 2307px;z-index: 98;;;;;;false;">的决定有可能是基于对事实的认识，也很有可能是基于情绪的变化；在交谈中，他</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-20" style="width: 4282px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9111px;left: 1429px;z-index: 99;;;;;;false;">们关注的是语气语调、隐射与暗示，而不是言语本来的含义。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9103px;left: 5715px;z-index: 100;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-0" style="width: 5814px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9359px;left: 1587px;z-index: 101;letter-spacing: -0.9199999999999999px;;;;;;false;">忧郁能带来甜蜜的遗憾。和抑郁一样，它们都产生于缺失感，但是在忧郁的情绪中，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-11" style="width: 634px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9359px;left: 7383px;z-index: 102;;;;;;false;">悲伤是美</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-0" style="width: 474px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9607px;left: 1429px;z-index: 103;;;;;;false;">好的，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-11" style="width: 2062px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9607px;left: 1878px;z-index: 104;;;;;;false;">如同一片荒凉海岸上的迷雾。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-14" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9607px;left: 3917px;z-index: 105;;;;;;null;">4</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-0" style="width: 3174px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9607px;left: 3997px;z-index: 106;letter-spacing: 0.6px;;;;;;false;">号性格者在情感变化的迷雾中感到强烈活力。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-5" style="width: 952px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9607px;left: 7146px;z-index: 107;;;;;;false;">在他们看来，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-21" style="width: 3330px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9855px;left: 1429px;z-index: 108;;;;;;false;">没有什么是永恒的，因为他们的情绪说变就变。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9847px;left: 4763px;z-index: 109;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-25" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10102px;left: 1512px;z-index: 110;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-25" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10102px;left: 1592px;z-index: 111;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-25" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10102px;left: 1672px;z-index: 112;;;;;;null;">4</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-28" style="width: 3502px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10102px;left: 1752px;z-index: 113;;;;;;false;">号性格者的核心问题是缺失感和时常降低的自尊。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-29" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 10094px;left: 5258px;z-index: 114;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-14" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10350px;left: 1429px;z-index: 115;;;;;;null;">4</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-21" style="width: 6503px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10350px;left: 1509px;z-index: 116;;;;;;false;">号性格者总是有意无意地把注意力放在遗失的美好上。拥有的东西看上去总是枯燥和毫无价值</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-0" style="width: 316px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10598px;left: 1429px;z-index: 117;;;;;;false;">的。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10590px;left: 1747px;z-index: 118;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-0" style="width: 316px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10845px;left: 1587px;z-index: 119;;;;;;false;">对于</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-14" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10845px;left: 1903px;z-index: 120;;;;;;null;">4</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-0" style="width: 6029px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10845px;left: 1983px;z-index: 121;letter-spacing: 0.53px;;;;;;false;">号来说，追求快乐可能让他们失去与内心情感世界的联系。更糟糕的是，他们担心自己</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-22" style="width: 3012px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11093px;left: 1429px;z-index: 122;;;;;;false;">会变得和他人毫无区别，过着平庸的生活。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11085px;left: 4445px;z-index: 123;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-27" style="width: 318px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11341px;left: 1429px;z-index: 124;letter-spacing: 1.7999999999999998px;;;;;;false;">二、</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-25" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11341px;left: 1749px;z-index: 125;;;;;;null;">4</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-27" style="width: 1589px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11341px;left: 1829px;z-index: 126;letter-spacing: 0.9099999999999999px;;;;;;false;">号性格者的主要特征：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11332px;left: 3422px;z-index: 127;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-11" style="width: 4760px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11588px;left: 1747px;z-index: 128;;;;;;false;">觉得有些东西在生活中遗失了，而别人又恰好拥有自己遗失的东西。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11580px;left: 6510px;z-index: 129;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-0" style="width: 4124px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11836px;left: 1747px;z-index: 130;letter-spacing: 0.52px;;;;;;false;">被遥不可及的事物深深吸引。把一个不存在的恋人理想化。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s6-6" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11828px;left: 5875px;z-index: 131;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p></div></div></div>

                <div class="ie-fix"><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-3" style="width: 5235px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1186px;left: 1747px;z-index: 2;;;;;;false;">依靠情绪、礼貌、华丽的外表和高雅的品味等外在表现来支撑自己的自尊。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 1178px;left: 6987px;z-index: 3;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-7" style="width: 4124px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1434px;left: 1747px;z-index: 4;;;;;;false;">带有忧郁感。追求的目标是深入的感情而不是纯粹的快乐。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 1425px;left: 5875px;z-index: 5;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;">

158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1681px;left: 2610px;z-index: 8;;;;;;false;">普遍情感的平淡</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-9" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1681px;left:
