reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 1673px;left: 8023px;z-index: 13;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-11" style="width: 5552px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1929px;left: 1747px;z-index: 14;;;;;;false;">追寻真实。感觉现实不是真的，相信当个人被真爱包围时，真正的自我将出现。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 1921px;left: 7305px;z-index: 15;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-12" style="width: 5393px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2177px;left: 1747px;z-index: 16;;;;;;false;">被生活中真实和激烈的事物所深深吸引，比如生死、性爱、灾难、遗弃等等。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2168px;left: 7145px;z-index: 17;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-13" style="width: 1108px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2424px;left: 1747px;z-index: 18;;;;;;false;">对已经拥有的，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-14" style="width: 952px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2424px;left: 2819px;z-index: 19;;;;;;false;">只看到缺点；</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-8" style="width: 1426px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2424px;left: 3733px;z-index: 20;;;;;;false;">对那些遥不可及的，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-15" style="width: 1110px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2424px;left: 5121px;z-index: 21;;;;;;false;">却能看到优点。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 1907px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2424px;left: 6195px;z-index: 22;letter-spacing: 0.8500000000000001px;;;;;;false;">这种变化的关注点加强了：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-15" style="width: 2062px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 1429px;z-index: 23;;;;;;false;">被抛弃的感觉和缺失的感觉。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2664px;left: 3492px;z-index: 24;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-16" style="width: 3806px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2920px;left: 1747px;z-index: 25;;;;;;false;">敏感于他人的情感和痛苦，能够帮助那些困境中的人。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2911px;left: 5557px;z-index: 26;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-15" style="width: 2538px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3167px;left: 1747px;z-index: 27;;;;;;false;">他们总是在哀悼生活中失去的东西。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-15" style="width: 3014px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3167px;left: 4247px;z-index: 28;;;;;;false;">他们的整个思想都被这种悲伤情绪所笼罩，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-8" style="width: 792px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3167px;left: 7223px;z-index: 29;;;;;;false;">以致于他们</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-16" style="width: 2220px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3415px;left: 1429px;z-index: 30;;;;;;false;">很难去关注那些更积极的事情。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3407px;left: 3652px;z-index: 31;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 474px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 1747px;z-index: 32;;;;;;false;">正常的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-17" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 2221px;z-index: 33;;;;;;null;">4</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-15" style="width: 4442px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 2301px;z-index: 34;;;;;;false;">号性格者说，如果生活开始变得糟糕，自杀的念头就会作为一种</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-9" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 6748px;z-index: 35;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 316px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 6817px;z-index: 36;;;;;;false;">选择</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-9" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 7133px;z-index: 37;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-8" style="width: 792px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 7206px;z-index: 38;;;;;;false;">出现在他们</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-8" style="width: 792px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3910px;left: 1429px;z-index: 39;;;;;;false;">的思想中。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3902px;left: 2223px;z-index: 40;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-17" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 4158px;left: 1429px;z-index: 41;;;;;;null;">4</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-16" style="width: 6345px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 4158px;left: 1509px;z-index: 42;;;;;;false;">号性格的情感生活总是处于巅峰或低谷中。他们倾向于在极度的抑郁和极度的亢奋中生活。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 4150px;left: 7859px;z-index: 43;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-7" style="width: 3648px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 1747px;z-index: 44;;;;;;false;">一个浪漫者可以完全陷入自己的空想中，满脑子都是</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-9" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 5399px;z-index: 45;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-13" 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 6579px;z-index: 47;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 474px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 6651px;z-index: 48;;;;;;false;">，或者</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-9" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 7127px;z-index: 49;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-8" style="width: 792px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 7198px;z-index: 50;;;;;;false;">他爱我又会</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 474px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 1429px;z-index: 51;;;;;;false;">怎么样</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-9" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 1903px;z-index: 52;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-14" style="width: 2540px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 1973px;z-index: 53;;;;;;false;">，以至于她根本不知道此时此刻她对</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-9" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 4517px;z-index: 54;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 158px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 4586px;z-index: 55;;;;;;null;">他</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-9" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 4744px;z-index: 56;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 952px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 4814px;z-index: 57;letter-spacing: 0.71px;;;;;;false;">的真实感觉。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4645px;left: 5769px;z-index: 58;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-21" style="width: 1273px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4901px;left: 1429px;z-index: 59;;;;;;false;">三、适合的环境：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4893px;left: 2703px;z-index: 60;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-8" style="width: 1426px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 1747px;z-index: 61;;;;;;false;">一般会有两种工作：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-9" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 3147px;z-index: 62;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-14" style="width: 2540px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 3216px;z-index: 63;;;;;;false;">养家糊口的工作和艺术家的真正工作</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-9" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 5757px;z-index: 64;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 158px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 5828px;z-index: 65;;;;;;null;">。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-15" style="width: 2062px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 5957px;z-index: 66;;;;;;false;">他们喜欢那些需要经过一定身</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-7" style="width: 6663px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5396px;left: 1429px;z-index: 67;;;;;;false;">体训练才能完成的工作，比如舞蹈演员、民谣女歌手、杂志模特。他们还可以成为画室的主人、</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-15" style="width: 3966px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5644px;left: 1429px;z-index: 68;;;;;;false;">室内装潢设计师、古董收集者和高品质二手商品的老板。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5636px;left: 5397px;z-index: 69;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-17" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 5892px;left: 1747px;z-index: 70;;;;;;null;">4</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 6185px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 5892px;left: 1827px;z-index: 71;letter-spacing: 0.47px;;;;;;false;">号性格者精通玄学，能够成为思想深邃的哲学家，他们寻找内心的高层境界。他们因此可</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-7" style="width: 6663px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6139px;left: 1429px;z-index: 72;;;;;;false;">以成为悲伤心理顾问、女权主义者和动物权利保护者。他们总是对宗教、仪式和艺术充满兴趣。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6131px;left: 8023px;z-index: 73;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-18" style="width: 1433px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6387px;left: 1429px;z-index: 74;letter-spacing: 1.23px;;;;;;false;">四、不适合的环境：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6379px;left: 2863px;z-index: 75;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-15" style="width: 2062px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6635px;left: 1747px;z-index: 76;;;;;;false;">包括普通环境下的世俗工作。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-9" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6635px;left: 3791px;z-index: 77;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 2359px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6635px;left: 3862px;z-index: 78;letter-spacing: -0.81px;;;;;;false;">我在办公室里工作，但那不是我。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-9" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6635px;left: 6204px;z-index: 79;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-12" style="width: 1744px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6635px;left: 6276px;z-index: 80;;;;;;false;">他们不适合和比他们更富</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-16" style="width: 6345px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6882px;left: 1429px;z-index: 81;;;;;;false;">有的人一起工作，也不适合服务性工作、默默无闻的工作，或者无法表现他们才华的工作。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6874px;left: 7779px;z-index: 82;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-22" style="width: 478px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7130px;left: 1429px;z-index: 83;;;;;;false;">五、对</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-24" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7130px;left: 1909px;z-index: 84;;;;;;null;">4</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-18" style="width: 1591px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7130px;left: 1987px;z-index: 85;letter-spacing: 1.09px;;;;;;false;">号性格者有利的做法：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7122px;left: 3580px;z-index: 86;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-16" style="width: 4282px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7378px;left: 1747px;z-index: 87;;;;;;false;">承认自己早期的缺失是真的；在悲伤之后，要把他放到一边。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7370px;left: 6034px;z-index: 88;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-25" style="width: 2378px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7626px;left: 1747px;z-index: 89;;;;;;false;">注意到当强烈的情感变化发生时，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 1588px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7626px;left: 4100px;z-index: 90;letter-spacing: 0.73px;;;;;;false;">自己会完全投入其中。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-15" style="width: 2062px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7626px;left: 5664px;z-index: 91;;;;;;false;">把注意力转移到其他事物上，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 316px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7626px;left: 7701px;z-index: 92;;;;;;false;">让自</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7873px;left: 1429px;z-index: 93;letter-spacing: 0.43999999999999995px;;;;;;false;">己从这种专注中解脱出来。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7865px;left: 3334px;z-index: 94;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-3" style="width: 5235px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8121px;left: 1747px;z-index: 95;;;;;;false;">养成善始善终的习惯。把被破坏或者被遗弃的工作当成未完成的工作做完。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8113px;left: 6987px;z-index: 96;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-3" style="width: 2696px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8368px;left: 1747px;z-index: 97;;;;;;false;">发现自己身上那些令他人羡慕的特质。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8360px;left: 4447px;z-index: 98;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-12" style="width: 4917px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8616px;left: 1747px;z-index: 99;;;;;;false;">与其可以追求快乐，不如坦然接受伤感。要知道这样的情绪总会过去。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8608px;left: 6668px;z-index: 100;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 950px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8864px;left: 1747px;z-index: 101;letter-spacing: 0.32px;;;;;;false;">让他人知道，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 1904px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8864px;left: 2672px;z-index: 102;letter-spacing: 0.59px;;;;;;false;">过度亲近会遭到你的攻击，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 1270px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8864px;left: 4552px;z-index: 103;letter-spacing: 0.7000000000000001px;;;;;;false;">请他们不要误会。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 2223px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8864px;left: 5797px;z-index: 104;letter-spacing: 0.75px;;;;;;false;">告诉他人在你生气的时候不要离</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-7" style="width: 4124px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9111px;left: 1429px;z-index: 105;;;;;;false;">去，这样你就会确信，即便他们受到攻击，也不会抛弃你。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9103px;left: 5557px;z-index: 106;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-11" style="width: 5076px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9359px;left: 1747px;z-index: 107;;;;;;false;">为自己能够感知他人的痛苦感到骄傲，但是要学会自如运用你的注意力。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9351px;left: 6828px;z-index: 108;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-3" style="width: 5711px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9607px;left: 1747px;z-index: 109;;;;;;false;">把注意力放在眼前。当注意力转移时，提醒自己。不要仅仅关注眼前的负面因素。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9598px;left: 7463px;z-index: 110;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-18" style="width: 5415px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9855px;left: 1749px;z-index: 111;letter-spacing: 1.1400000000000001px;;;;;;false;">培养多样的兴趣，结交各种朋友，把自己的注意力从抑郁的情绪中转移出来。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-26" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9847px;left: 7169px;z-index: 112;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-21" style="width: 2389px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10102px;left: 1749px;z-index: 113;;;;;;false;">通过身体的运动练习来调节心情。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-26" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10094px;left: 4140px;z-index: 114;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-12" style="width: 4917px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10350px;left: 1747px;z-index: 115;;;;;;false;">当真实的感受被强烈的情感掩盖时，要注意到这一点，尤其是当你感到</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-9" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10350px;left: 6668px;z-index: 116;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-25" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10350px;left: 6739px;z-index: 117;;;;;;false;">一切又会变得很糟</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 158px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10598px;left: 1429px;z-index: 118;;;;;;null;">糕</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-9" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10598px;left: 1587px;z-index: 119;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 316px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10598px;left: 1657px;z-index: 120;;;;;;false;">时。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10590px;left: 1975px;z-index: 121;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-22" style="width: 318px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10845px;left: 1429px;z-index: 122;;;;;;false;">六、</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-24" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10845px;left: 1749px;z-index: 123;;;;;;null;">4</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-18" style="width: 1909px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10845px;left: 1829px;z-index: 124;letter-spacing: 1.04px;;;;;;false;">号性格者需要注意的做法：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10837px;left: 3740px;z-index: 125;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-16" style="width: 4282px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11093px;left: 1747px;z-index: 126;;;;;;false;">对摆在眼前的问题想尽各种解决方法，尝试各种解决途径，但</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-18" style="width: 1912px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11093px;left: 6032px;z-index: 127;letter-spacing: 1.34px;;;;;;false;">就是不愿意采取实质行动，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-18" style="width: 1116px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11341px;left: 1429px;z-index: 128;letter-spacing: 1.49px;;;;;;false;">推动事物发展。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-26" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11332px;left: 2545px;z-index: 129;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-15" style="width: 1110px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11588px;left: 1747px;z-index: 130;;;;;;false;">不喜欢被分类，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 2856px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11588px;left: 2819px;z-index: 131;letter-spacing: 0.5800000000000001px;;;;;;false;">不喜欢别人把自己的问题看成普遍问题。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-25" style="width: 2378px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11588px;left: 5637px;z-index: 132;;;;;;false;">认为他人没有理解情况的独特性和</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-1" style="width: 632px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11836px;left: 1429px;z-index: 133;;;;;;false;">严重性。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s7-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11828px;left: 2063px;z-index: 134;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p></div></div></div>

</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-17" style="width: 2697px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 1747px;z-index: 36;;;;;;false;">把自己和他人比较，嫉妒他人的优点。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-5" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 4447px;z-index: 37;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-16" style="width: 952px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 4515px;z-index: 38;;;;;;false;">她比我漂亮。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-5" style="width: 142px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 5468px;z-index: 39;letter-spacing: 2.06px;;;;;;false;">”“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-1" style="width: 1270px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 5609px;z-index: 40;letter-spacing: 0.7000000000000001px;;;;;;false;">他的衣服比我好。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-5" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 6880px;z-index: 41;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2664px;left: 6952px;z-index: 42;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-18" style="width: 3808px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2920px;left: 1747px;z-index: 43;;;;;;false;">诱惑和拒绝。在对方拒绝你之前，先找到对方的缺点。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2911px;left: 5557px;z-index: 44;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-1" style="width: 4562px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3167px;left: 1747px;z-index: 45;letter-spacing: -0.75px;;;;;;false;">强烈的自我批评。对自己的形象产生错误的判断，觉得毫无优点。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-12" style="width: 1428px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3167px;left: 6291px;z-index: 46;;;;;;false;">总是觉得自己太胖，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-1" style="width: 317px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3167px;left: 7700px;z-index: 47;letter-spacing: 1.6400000000000001px;;;;;;false;">常常</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-1" style="width: 1744px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3415px;left: 1429px;z-index: 48;letter-spacing: 0.49px;;;;;;false;">出现厌食或易饿的症状。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3407px;left: 3176px;z-index: 49;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-19" style="width: 4124px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 1747px;z-index: 50;;;;;;false;">言语尖锐，讽刺他人。觉得是他人的错误导致了你的痛苦。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3654px;left: 5875px;z-index: 51;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-19" style="width: 4124px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3910px;left: 1747px;z-index: 52;;;;;;false;">寻求他人的建议，然后拒绝采用。不愿放弃受害者的形象。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3902px;left: 5875px;z-index: 53;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 4154px;left: 1429px;z-index: 54;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-20" style="width: 668px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4626px;left: 1429px;z-index: 55;letter-spacing: -0.5800000000000001px;;;;;;false;">九型人格</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 83px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4626px;left: 2097px;z-index: 56;;;;;;null;">5</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-20" style="width: 1834px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4626px;left: 2179px;z-index: 57;letter-spacing: -0.8699999999999999px;;;;;;false;">号性格－－研究型、理性</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4626px;left: 4012px;z-index: 58;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 1242px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 5093px;left: 1429px;z-index: 59;letter-spacing: -0.32px;;;;;;false;">2008-07-20 10:13 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-1" style="width: 632px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5568px;left: 1429px;z-index: 60;;;;;;false;">九型人格</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-21" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5568px;left: 2061px;z-index: 61;;;;;;null;">5</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-16" style="width: 952px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5568px;left: 2141px;z-index: 62;;;;;;false;">号领导特质：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5560px;left: 3096px;z-index: 63;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-21" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 5816px;left: 1429px;z-index: 64;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-21" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 5816px;left: 1509px;z-index: 65;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-21" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 5816px;left: 1589px;z-index: 66;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-18 reader-word-s8-22" style="width: 6347px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 5816px;left: 1669px;z-index: 67;letter-spacing: 0.56px;;;;;;false;">理性、喜欢研究、像大学教授、书香味很浓、不喜欢同人打交道、不大讲究外表。但自我会</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-22" style="width: 955px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6063px;left: 1429px;z-index: 68;letter-spacing: 1.31px;;;;;;false;">有一种优越感</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-1" style="width: 158px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6063px;left: 2387px;z-index: 69;;;;;;null;">。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6055px;left: 2543px;z-index: 70;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-26" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 6311px;left: 1429px;z-index: 71;;;;;;null;">5</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-22" style="width: 1273px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 6311px;left: 1509px;z-index: 72;letter-spacing: 1.21px;;;;;;false;">号性格才力：智将</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-8 reader-word-s8-25" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 6303px;left: 2783px;z-index: 73;font-size: 167px;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-14 reader-word-s8-22" style="width: 638px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6558px;left: 1429px;z-index: 74;letter-spacing: 1.79px;;;;;;false;">一、困境</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6550px;left: 2067px;z-index: 75;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-27" style="width: 1584px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6806px;left: 1747px;z-index: 76;;;;;;false;">他们是非常私密的人。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6798px;left: 3334px;z-index: 77;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-1" style="width: 2536px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7054px;left: 1747px;z-index: 78;letter-spacing: 0.42999999999999994px;;;;;;false;">他们喜欢呆在家里，把电话线拔掉。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7046px;left: 4287px;z-index: 79;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-1" style="width: 3012px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7302px;left: 1747px;z-index: 80;letter-spacing: 0.44999999999999996px;;;;;;false;">他们喜欢与世隔绝，不受感情问题的困扰。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7293px;left: 4763px;z-index: 81;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-4" style="width: 3806px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7549px;left: 1747px;z-index: 82;;;;;;false;">当他人积极投入时，他们却像旁观者一样，无动于衷。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7541px;left: 5557px;z-index: 83;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-21" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7797px;left: 1747px;z-index: 84;;;;;;null;">5</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-28" style="width: 6185px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7797px;left: 1827px;z-index: 85;;;;;;false;">号性格者不需要言语，就能感觉到与他人紧密联系。在两性关系中，他们仅需要很少的接</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-29" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8045px;left: 1429px;z-index: 86;;;;;;false;">触，就能把关系维持下去。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8036px;left: 3334px;z-index: 87;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-22" style="width: 318px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8292px;left: 1429px;z-index: 88;letter-spacing: 1.7999999999999998px;;;;;;false;">二、</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-26" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8292px;left: 1749px;z-index: 89;;;;;;null;">5</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-22" style="width: 1589px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8292px;left: 1829px;z-index: 90;letter-spacing: 0.9099999999999999px;;;;;;false;">号性格者的主要特征：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8284px;left: 3422px;z-index: 91;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-1" style="width: 474px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8540px;left: 1747px;z-index: 92;;;;;;false;">私密。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8532px;left: 2223px;z-index: 93;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-1" style="width: 5076px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8788px;left: 1747px;z-index: 94;letter-spacing: 0.53px;;;;;;false;">保持不被涉及的状态；感到威胁时，第一道防线是撤退或者系紧安全带。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8779px;left: 6828px;z-index: 95;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-15" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9035px;left: 1747px;z-index: 96;;;;;;false;">害怕用心去感觉。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9027px;left: 3018px;z-index: 97;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-10" style="width: 3172px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9283px;left: 1747px;z-index: 98;;;;;;false;">过度强调自我控制。把注意力从感觉上挪开。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-5" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9283px;left: 4923px;z-index: 99;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-13" style="width: 1904px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9283px;left: 4992px;z-index: 100;;;;;;false;">戏剧是给那些普通人看的。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-5" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9283px;left: 6897px;z-index: 101;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9275px;left: 6969px;z-index: 102;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-17" style="width: 5078px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9530px;left: 1747px;z-index: 103;;;;;;false;">情感延迟。在他人面前控制感觉，等到自己一个人的时候，才表露情感。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9522px;left: 6828px;z-index: 104;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-10" style="width: 6187px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9779px;left: 1747px;z-index: 105;;;;;;false;">把生活划分成不同的区域。把不同的事情放在不同的盒子里，给每个盒子一个时间限制。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9770px;left: 7939px;z-index: 106;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-15" style="width: 2378px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10026px;left: 1747px;z-index: 107;;;;;;false;">希望能够预测到将要发生的事情。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10018px;left: 4128px;z-index: 108;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-6" style="width: 5870px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10274px;left: 1747px;z-index: 109;;;;;;false;">对那些解释人类行为的特殊知识和分析系统感兴趣。希望找到一张解释情感的地图。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10266px;left: 7621px;z-index: 110;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-19" style="width: 4600px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10521px;left: 1747px;z-index: 111;;;;;;false;">分不清精神上的不依赖和拒绝痛苦的情感封闭，是没有悟道的佛。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10513px;left: 6352px;z-index: 112;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-19" style="width: 3648px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10769px;left: 1747px;z-index: 113;;;;;;false;">喜欢从一个旁观者的角度来关注自己和自己的生活，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-1" style="width: 794px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10769px;left: 5357px;z-index: 114;letter-spacing: 0.8200000000000001px;;;;;;false;">这将导致：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-29" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10769px;left: 6113px;z-index: 115;;;;;;false;">与自己生活中的事件和情感</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-10" style="width: 3172px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11017px;left: 1429px;z-index: 116;;;;;;false;">隔离；能让自己的观点不受情感偏见的影响。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11009px;left: 4605px;z-index: 117;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-21" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11264px;left: 1747px;z-index: 118;;;;;;null;">5</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-28" style="width: 6185px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11264px;left: 1827px;z-index: 119;;;;;;false;">号性格者希望提前知道任何会让他们感到尴尬的时刻。任何意料之外的事情，任何来自他</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-27" style="width: 1584px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11512px;left: 1429px;z-index: 120;;;;;;false;">人的强烈要求，都会让</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-21" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11512px;left: 3014px;z-index: 121;;;;;;null;">5</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-16" style="width: 952px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11512px;left: 3094px;z-index: 122;;;;;;false;">号慌乱不堪。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11504px;left: 4048px;z-index: 123;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-1" style="width: 158px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11760px;left: 1747px;z-index: 124;;;;;;null;">当</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-21" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11760px;left: 1905px;z-index: 125;;;;;;null;">5</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-1" style="width: 792px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11760px;left: 1985px;z-index: 126;letter-spacing: 0.41000000000000003px;;;;;;false;">号独处时，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-6" style="width: 1110px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11760px;left: 2752px;z-index: 127;;;;;;false;">他们充满幻想，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-10" style="width: 2696px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11760px;left: 3838px;z-index: 128;;;;;;false;">他们会去思考那些他们感兴趣的事物。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-21" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11760px;left: 6512px;z-index: 129;;;;;;null;">5</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-12" style="width: 1428px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11760px;left: 6592px;z-index: 130;;;;;;false;">号性格者喜欢与自己</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-1" style="width: 950px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 12007px;left: 1429px;z-index: 131;letter-spacing: 0.32px;;;;;;false;">的心灵做伴，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-6" style="width: 3014px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 12007px;left: 2343px;z-index: 132;;;;;;false;">除非这种独处发展成了与世隔绝的孤独感，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s8-10" style="width: 2696px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 12007px;left: 5319px;z-index: 133;;;;;;false;">否则他们很少会在独处的时候感到沮丧
</p></div></div></div>

                <div class="ie-fix"><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-3" style="width: 1108px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1186px;left: 1429px;z-index: 2;;;;;;false;">或者无所事事。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 1178px;left: 2539px;z-index: 3;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-10" style="width: 1273px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1434px;left: 1429px;z-index: 4;;;;;;false;">三、适合的环境：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 1425px;left: 2703px;z-index: 5;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-12" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 1681px;left: 1749px;z-index: 6;;;;;;null;">5</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-8" style="width: 6189px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 1681px;left: 1829px;z-index: 7;letter-spacing: 0.56px;;;;;;false;">号性格者会成为出色的学者，他们研究的领域往往是晦涩难懂，但却非常重要的。他们会</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-8" style="width: 6529px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1929px;left: 1429px;z-index: 8;letter-spacing: 1.1px;;;;;;false;">成为这些领域的佼佼者，比如为心理学家提供心理服务的心理学家等。他们的著作可能只是薄</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-13" style="width: 3184px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2177px;left: 1429px;z-index: 9;;;;;;false;">薄的一本，但往往却浓缩了毕生研究的精华。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-14" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2168px;left: 4616px;z-index: 10;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-10" style="width: 3504px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2424px;left: 1749px;z-index: 11;;;;;;false;">他们会是那些古老语言的活字典，常常学富五车。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-1" style="width: 2692px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2424px;left: 5258px;z-index: 12;letter-spacing: 0.29000000000000004px;;;;;;false;">他们也可以成为那些喜欢在业工作的电</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-15" style="width: 3966px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 1429px;z-index: 13;;;;;;false;">脑程序员，或者是那些在股票交易所控制股票市场的人。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2664px;left: 5397px;z-index: 14;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-8" style="width: 1433px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2920px;left: 1429px;z-index: 15;letter-spacing: 1.23px;;;;;;false;">四、不适合的环境：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2911px;left: 2863px;z-index: 16;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-1" style="width: 3012px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3167px;left: 1747px;z-index: 17;letter-spacing: 0.44999999999999996px;;;;;;false;">任何需要公开竞争或者直接接触的工作都是</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-16" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3167px;left: 4761px;z-index: 18;;;;;;null;">5</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-17" style="width: 3172px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3167px;left: 4841px;z-index: 19;;;;;;false;">号所不喜欢的，比如销售人员、公共政策讨论</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-1" style="width: 2536px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3415px;left: 1429px;z-index: 20;letter-spacing: 0.42999999999999994px;;;;;;false;">者、要时刻面带微笑的政党候选人。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3407px;left: 3968px;z-index: 21;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-18" style="width: 478px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 1429px;z-index: 22;;;;;;false;">五、对</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-12" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 1909px;z-index: 23;;;;;;null;">5</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-19" style="width: 1113px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 1987px;z-index: 24;;;;;;false;">号有利的做法：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3654px;left: 3102px;z-index: 25;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-20" style="width: 3806px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3910px;left: 1747px;z-index: 26;;;;;;false;">注意到他人在期待回应时，自己却有刻意保留的欲望。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-21" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3910px;left: 5557px;z-index: 27;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-22" style="width: 2380px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3910px;left: 5626px;z-index: 28;;;;;;false;">我什么时候想做就会做，而不是你</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-3" style="width: 1108px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4158px;left: 1429px;z-index: 29;;;;;;false;">让我做我就做。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-21" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4158px;left: 2537px;z-index: 30;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4150px;left: 2610px;z-index: 31;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-23" style="width: 4600px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 1747px;z-index: 32;;;;;;false;">不要让情感被理性分析所取代，不要让精神建构替代了真实经验。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4398px;left: 6352px;z-index: 33;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-8" style="width: 2548px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 1749px;z-index: 34;letter-spacing: 1.2px;;;;;;false;">认识到接触情感并不等于受到伤害。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-14" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4645px;left: 4300px;z-index: 35;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-13" style="width: 3184px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4901px;left: 1749px;z-index: 36;;;;;;false;">认识到自己渴望得到认可，又不想花费力气。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-14" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4893px;left: 4936px;z-index: 37;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-24" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 1747px;z-index: 38;;;;;;false;">认识到自己总是离不开三个</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-16" style="width: 87px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 3692px;z-index: 39;;;;;;null;">S</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-1" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 3820px;z-index: 40;letter-spacing: 0.53px;;;;;;false;">的陪伴？：秘密（</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-16" style="width: 526px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 5089px;z-index: 41;;;;;;false;">secrecy)</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-1" style="width: 632px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 5618px;z-index: 42;;;;;;false;">、优越（</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-16" style="width: 737px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 6253px;z-index: 43;;;;;;false;">superiority)</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-1" style="width: 474px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 6994px;z-index: 44;;;;;;false;">和分离</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-16" style="width: 936px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 5396px;left: 1429px;z-index: 45;;;;;;false;">(separateness).</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 5388px;left: 2368px;z-index: 46;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-8" style="width: 4937px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5644px;left: 1749px;z-index: 47;letter-spacing: 1.1500000000000001px;;;;;;false;">学会接受突发情况。学会去冒险，去求助，去让私下的梦想变成现实。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-14" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5636px;left: 6691px;z-index: 48;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-25" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5892px;left: 1747px;z-index: 49;;;;;;false;">与他人在一起时，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-1" style="width: 1428px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5892px;left: 2990px;z-index: 50;letter-spacing: 0.61px;;;;;;false;">自己能感受到什么，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-15" style="width: 3014px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5892px;left: 4394px;z-index: 51;;;;;;false;">把这种感受与自己独处时的感受进行对比，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-1" style="width: 632px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5892px;left: 7385px;z-index: 52;;;;;;false;">找到两种</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-26" style="width: 950px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6139px;left: 1429px;z-index: 53;;;;;;false;">感受的差异。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6131px;left: 2381px;z-index: 54;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-25" style="width: 3488px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6387px;left: 1747px;z-index: 55;;;;;;false;">学会坚持完成重要的项目，并且把他们公之于众。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-8" style="width: 1914px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6387px;left: 5237px;z-index: 56;letter-spacing: 1.5px;;;;;;false;">让自己的成果被他人看见。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6379px;left: 7154px;z-index: 57;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-20" style="width: 2220px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6635px;left: 1747px;z-index: 58;;;;;;false;">对最简单的物质生活提出质疑。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6626px;left: 3970px;z-index: 59;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-20" style="width: 2220px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6882px;left: 1747px;z-index: 60;;;;;;false;">学会从自己的特殊研究中受益。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6874px;left: 3970px;z-index: 61;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-15" style="width: 2062px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7130px;left: 1747px;z-index: 62;;;;;;false;">学会容忍他人的需要和情感。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7122px;left: 3810px;z-index: 63;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-19" style="width: 5891px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7378px;left: 1749px;z-index: 64;;;;;;false;">愿意当场表现自己的情感，可以通过格式塔心理学、身体练习或者艺术工作来表现。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-1" style="width: 316px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7378px;left: 7648px;z-index: 65;;;;;;false;">但是</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-26" style="width: 950px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7626px;left: 1429px;z-index: 66;;;;;;false;">同时要注意，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-8" style="width: 3507px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7626px;left: 2379px;z-index: 67;letter-spacing: 1.31px;;;;;;false;">不要在不成熟的情况下，让自己的情感一泻千里。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-3" style="width: 2058px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7626px;left: 5891px;z-index: 68;;;;;;false;">允许延迟的情感反应与直觉发</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-1" style="width: 632px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7873px;left: 1429px;z-index: 69;;;;;;false;">生联系。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7865px;left: 2063px;z-index: 70;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-18" style="width: 318px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8121px;left: 1429px;z-index: 71;;;;;;false;">六、</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-12" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8121px;left: 1749px;z-index: 72;;;;;;null;">5</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-8" style="width: 1431px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8121px;left: 1829px;z-index: 73;letter-spacing: 1.02px;;;;;;false;">号需要注意的做法：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8113px;left: 3262px;z-index: 74;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-20" style="width: 2220px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8368px;left: 1747px;z-index: 75;;;;;;false;">让自己离开身体，退缩到内心。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8360px;left: 3970px;z-index: 76;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-23" style="width: 3648px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8616px;left: 1747px;z-index: 77;;;;;;false;">希望储藏时间和精力。总是在节省，而不是在付出。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8608px;left: 5399px;z-index: 78;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-20" style="width: 4282px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8864px;left: 1747px;z-index: 79;;;;;;false;">难以展现自我。把暴露自我的话从对话中过滤掉。保留信息。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8856px;left: 6034px;z-index: 80;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-17" style="width: 2696px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9111px;left: 1747px;z-index: 81;;;;;;false;">不愿给予；感觉被他人的需求所利用。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9103px;left: 4447px;z-index: 82;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-24" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9359px;left: 1747px;z-index: 83;;;;;;false;">过于自负，不愿依赖他人。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-21" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9359px;left: 3652px;z-index: 84;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-15" style="width: 1110px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9359px;left: 3721px;z-index: 85;;;;;;false;">没你我也可以。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-21" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9359px;left: 4832px;z-index: 86;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9351px;left: 4904px;z-index: 87;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-27" style="width: 2854px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9607px;left: 1747px;z-index: 88;;;;;;false;">对承诺感到疲惫。不愿与他人分享太多。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9598px;left: 4605px;z-index: 89;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-17" style="width: 6187px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9855px;left: 1747px;z-index: 90;;;;;;false;">用思想取代现实体验。不断巩固孤独者的立场。幻想不切实际的生活，而不是面对现实。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9847px;left: 7939px;z-index: 91;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-17" style="width: 3172px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10102px;left: 1747px;z-index: 92;;;;;;false;">幻想天上掉馅饼，可以不费力气就得到认可。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-21" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10102px;left: 4923px;z-index: 93;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-22" style="width: 2380px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10102px;left: 4992px;z-index: 94;;;;;;false;">如果上帝想要我，他就会来找我。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-21" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10102px;left: 7375px;z-index: 95;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10094px;left: 7446px;z-index: 96;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-1" style="width: 5871px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10350px;left: 1747px;z-index: 97;letter-spacing: 0.55px;;;;;;false;">把自己隐藏在一个表面的姿态里。让自己的表现适应周围环境，以避免被他人注意。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10342px;left: 7621px;z-index: 98;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-1" style="width: 2525px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10598px;left: 1747px;z-index: 99;letter-spacing: -0.27px;;;;;;false;">相信自己高人一等，不受感情控制。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-21" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10598px;left: 4262px;z-index: 100;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-15" style="width: 1586px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10598px;left: 4331px;z-index: 101;;;;;;false;">生气是愚蠢者的行为。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-21" style="width: 142px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10598px;left: 5904px;z-index: 102;letter-spacing: 2.06px;;;;;;false;">”“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-24" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10598px;left: 6047px;z-index: 103;;;;;;false;">他们为什么不能控制自己？</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-21" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10598px;left: 7951px;z-index: 104;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10590px;left: 8023px;z-index: 105;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-23" style="width: 4124px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10845px;left: 1747px;z-index: 106;;;;;;false;">害怕欲望而麻痹自己。让自己无法走出去，也无法退回来。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10837px;left: 5875px;z-index: 107;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-27" style="width: 2854px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11093px;left: 1747px;z-index: 108;;;;;;false;">脱离感情生活。喜欢私密，没有人知道。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11085px;left: 4605px;z-index: 109;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-20" style="width: 4282px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11341px;left: 1747px;z-index: 110;;;;;;false;">无法分清楚什么是精神上的舍弃，什么是对情感痛苦的逃避。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11332px;left: 6034px;z-index: 111;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s9-4" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 11584px;left: 1429px;z-index: 112;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p></div></div></div>

</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-12" style="width: 158px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5244px;left: 1747px;z-index: 34;;;;;;null;">当</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-19" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5244px;left: 1905px;z-index: 35;;;;;;null;">6</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-20" style="width: 6027px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5244px;left: 1985px;z-index: 36;;;;;;false;">号性格者感觉到内心受到威胁时，他们对外界的关注反而会变得更加强烈。内心越是痛</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-21" style="width: 5393px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5492px;left: 1429px;z-index: 37;;;;;;false;">苦，他们就越是喜欢往外看，结果常常让他们找错了让他们感到警惕的原因。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5483px;left: 6826px;z-index: 38;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-14" style="width: 318px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5739px;left: 1429px;z-index: 39;letter-spacing: 1.7999999999999998px;;;;;;false;">二、</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-15 reader-word-s10-22" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5739px;left: 1749px;z-index: 40;font-size: 158px;;;;;;null;">6</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-14" style="width: 1589px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5739px;left: 1829px;z-index: 41;letter-spacing: 0.9099999999999999px;;;;;;false;">号性格者的主要特征：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5731px;left: 3422px;z-index: 42;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-14" style="width: 2069px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5987px;left: 1749px;z-index: 43;letter-spacing: 1.09px;;;;;;false;">推延行动。用思想代替行动。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-11 reader-word-s10-22" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5979px;left: 3822px;z-index: 44;font-size: 167px;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-23" style="width: 1426px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6235px;left: 1747px;z-index: 45;;;;;;false;">工作无法善始善终。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6226px;left: 3176px;z-index: 46;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-24" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6482px;left: 1747px;z-index: 47;;;;;;false;">忘记对成功和快乐的追求。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6474px;left: 3652px;z-index: 48;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-25" style="width: 3012px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6730px;left: 1747px;z-index: 49;;;;;;false;">对权威的极端态度：要么顺从，要么反抗。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6722px;left: 4763px;z-index: 50;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-25" style="width: 3012px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6978px;left: 1747px;z-index: 51;;;;;;false;">怀疑他人的动机，尤其是权威人士的动机。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6970px;left: 4763px;z-index: 52;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-17" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7225px;left: 1747px;z-index: 53;;;;;;false;">认同被压迫者的反抗事业。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7217px;left: 3652px;z-index: 54;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-12" style="width: 3648px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7473px;left: 1747px;z-index: 55;letter-spacing: 0.52px;;;;;;false;">对于被压迫者或者强大的领导者表现出忠诚和责任。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7465px;left: 5399px;z-index: 56;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-25" style="width: 3012px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7721px;left: 1747px;z-index: 57;;;;;;false;">害怕直接发火。把自己的怒气归罪于别人。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7713px;left: 4763px;z-index: 58;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-23" style="width: 792px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7968px;left: 1747px;z-index: 59;;;;;;false;">疑心很重。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7960px;left: 2541px;z-index: 60;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-25" style="width: 3012px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8216px;left: 1747px;z-index: 61;;;;;;false;">在环境中搜索能够解释内在恐惧感的线索。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8208px;left: 4763px;z-index: 62;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-18" style="width: 5711px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8464px;left: 1747px;z-index: 63;;;;;;false;">通过强大的想象力和专一的注意力来获得直觉，这两种能力都来自于内心的恐惧。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8456px;left: 7463px;z-index: 64;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-19" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8711px;left: 1747px;z-index: 65;;;;;;null;">6</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-12" style="width: 790px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8711px;left: 1827px;z-index: 66;;;;;;false;">号性格者的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-14" style="width: 5400px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8711px;left: 2618px;z-index: 67;letter-spacing: 0.71px;;;;;;false;">家庭背景往往都是这样一个共同的主题：一个感觉无法保护自己的孩子，找不</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-14" style="width: 6529px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8959px;left: 1429px;z-index: 68;letter-spacing: 1.1px;;;;;;false;">到安全的藏身之地。这种家庭背景导致他们成年后，依然觉得自己属于受害者，找不到一个强</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-16" style="width: 1433px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9207px;left: 1429px;z-index: 69;;;;;;false;">大力量来保护自己。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9198px;left: 2863px;z-index: 70;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-19" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 9454px;left: 1747px;z-index: 71;;;;;;null;">6</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-26" style="width: 6185px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 9454px;left: 1827px;z-index: 72;;;;;;false;">号性格者拥有丰富的想象力，但是这种想象力对他们来说，既是福，又是祸。想象力导致</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-24" style="width: 1585px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9702px;left: 1429px;z-index: 73;;;;;;false;">了他们多疑的世界观。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9694px;left: 3016px;z-index: 74;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-19" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 9950px;left: 1747px;z-index: 75;;;;;;null;">6</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-26" style="width: 6185px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 9950px;left: 1827px;z-index: 76;;;;;;false;">号以为他们是为了保护自己而对周围环境进行扫描，而实际上他们不过是为了证实自己观</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-12" style="width: 6029px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10198px;left: 1429px;z-index: 77;letter-spacing: 0.53px;;;;;;false;">点；他们不是在寻找潜在危险，而是在寻找支持某个观点的证据。这种表现就是所谓的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-27" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10198px;left: 7463px;z-index: 78;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-12" style="width: 476px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10198px;left: 7531px;z-index: 79;letter-spacing: 0.8200000000000001px;;;;;;false;">投影作</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-12" style="width: 158px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10445px;left: 1429px;z-index: 80;;;;;;null;">用</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-27" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10445px;left: 1587px;z-index: 81;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-12" style="width: 158px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10445px;left: 1657px;z-index: 82;;;;;;null;">。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10437px;left: 1817px;z-index: 83;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-27" style="width: 70px;height: 175px;line-height: 175px;top: 10688px;left: 1747px;z-index: 84;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-12" style="width: 634px;height: 175px;line-height: 175px;top: 10688px;left: 1815px;z-index: 85;letter-spacing: 0.54px;;;;;;false;">逆流而上</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-27" style="width: 70px;height: 175px;line-height: 175px;top: 10688px;left: 2450px;z-index: 86;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-12" style="width: 1904px;height: 175px;line-height: 175px;top: 10688px;left: 2522px;z-index: 87;letter-spacing: 0.59px;;;;;;false;">这个词最能描述这种性格。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-12" style="width: 3174px;height: 175px;line-height: 175px;top: 10688px;left: 4398px;z-index: 88;letter-spacing: 0.6px;;;;;;false;">当你和社会认可的形象和行为都相距甚远时，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-12" style="width: 474px;height: 175px;line-height: 175px;top: 10688px;left: 7543px;z-index: 89;;;;;;false;">你就有</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-21" style="width: 4917px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10941px;left: 1429px;z-index: 90;;;;;;false;">了一种身份，你的任务就是回击强大的反对势力，让你的声音被听见。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10932px;left: 6350px;z-index: 91;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-19" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11188px;left: 1429px;z-index: 92;;;;;;null;">6</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-20" style="width: 5551px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11188px;left: 1509px;z-index: 93;;;;;;false;">号就是这么奇怪，当别人都在努力获得成功时，他们却在想方设法地避免成功。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-0" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 11180px;left: 7065px;z-index: 94;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-14" style="width: 1273px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11436px;left: 1429px;z-index: 95;letter-spacing: 1.1700000000000002px;;;;;;false;">三、适合的环境：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-0" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11428px;left: 2703px;z-index: 96;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-19" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11683px;left: 1747px;z-index: 97;;;;;;null;">6</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-26" style="width: 6185px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 11683px;left: 1827px;z-index: 98;;;;;;false;">号性格者喜欢等级分明的环境，权力、责任和问题都一清二楚。他们可以从事警务工作，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-12" style="width: 3649px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11931px;left: 1429px;z-index: 99;letter-spacing: 0.55px;;;;;;false;">也可以到大学攻读研究生课程。一个处于权威地位的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-19" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11931px;left: 5079px;z-index: 100;;;;;;null;">6</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s10-20" style="width: 2854px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11931px;left: 5159px;z-index: 101;;;;;;false;">号，要么会完全按照规章制度办事，要么
</p></div></div></div>
