                <div class="ie-fix"><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-3" style="width: 3806px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1186px;left: 1429px;z-index: 2;;;;;;false;">则站在反权威的立场上组织大家反对现有的规章制度。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-4" style="width: 2062px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1186px;left: 5199px;z-index: 3;;;;;;false;">他们还喜欢自己给自己干活，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-5" style="width: 792px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1186px;left: 7223px;z-index: 4;;;;;;false;">这样就不必</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-6" style="width: 1744px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1434px;left: 1429px;z-index: 5;;;;;;false;">受到领导或老板的控制。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 1425px;left: 3176px;z-index: 6;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-5" style="width: 792px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1681px;left: 1747px;z-index: 7;;;;;;false;">恐惧症型的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-9" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1681px;left: 2539px;z-index: 8;;;;;;null;">6</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-6" style="width: 5393px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1681px;left: 2620px;z-index: 9;;;;;;false;">号喜欢没有竞争压力的工作，愿意躲在一个强大的领导后面工作。反恐惧症型</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-0" style="width: 158px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1929px;left: 1429px;z-index: 10;;;;;;null;">的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-9" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1929px;left: 1587px;z-index: 11;;;;;;null;">6</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-3" style="width: 6345px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1929px;left: 1667px;z-index: 12;;;;;;false;">号则喜欢从事具有身体危险或者为被压迫者服务的工作。他们可以是桥梁的维修员，也可以</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-10" style="width: 3012px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2177px;left: 1429px;z-index: 13;;;;;;false;">是出色的商场战略家，帮助公司扭亏为盈。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-9" style="width: 39px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2177px;left: 4443px;z-index: 14;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2168px;left: 4525px;z-index: 15;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-11" style="width: 1433px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2424px;left: 1429px;z-index: 16;letter-spacing: 1.23px;;;;;;false;">四、不适合的环境：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2416px;left: 2863px;z-index: 17;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-9" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 2672px;left: 1747px;z-index: 18;;;;;;null;">6</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-13" style="width: 2854px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 2672px;left: 1827px;z-index: 19;;;;;;false;">号不喜欢的工作包括那些具有强大压力，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-14" style="width: 1904px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 2672px;left: 4643px;z-index: 20;;;;;;false;">需要在毫无准备的情况下，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-4" style="width: 1586px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 2672px;left: 6509px;z-index: 21;;;;;;false;">现场制定决策的工作。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-0" style="width: 4125px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2920px;left: 1429px;z-index: 22;letter-spacing: 0.56px;;;;;;false;">他们也不喜欢那些需要和他人竞争、背后勾心斗角的工作。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2911px;left: 5557px;z-index: 23;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-15" style="width: 478px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3167px;left: 1429px;z-index: 24;;;;;;false;">五、对</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-16" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3167px;left: 1909px;z-index: 25;;;;;;null;">6</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-11" style="width: 1273px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3167px;left: 1987px;z-index: 26;letter-spacing: 1.1700000000000002px;;;;;;false;">号有帮助的做法：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3159px;left: 3262px;z-index: 27;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-4" style="width: 2538px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3415px;left: 1747px;z-index: 28;;;;;;false;">学会通过现实来检验自己的畏惧感。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-0" style="width: 1270px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3415px;left: 4247px;z-index: 29;letter-spacing: 0.7000000000000001px;;;;;;false;">检查所有的事实。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-17" style="width: 2536px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3415px;left: 5481px;z-index: 30;;;;;;false;">把内心的害怕告诉一个值得信任的朋</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-18" style="width: 4124px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 1429px;z-index: 31;;;;;;false;">友，听听对方的反应，用事实结果来检验自己的思维判断。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3654px;left: 5557px;z-index: 32;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-4" style="width: 3490px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3910px;left: 1429px;z-index: 33;;;;;;false;">注意自己有从他人的行为中寻找潜在企图的习惯。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-4" style="width: 1586px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3910px;left: 4881px;z-index: 34;;;;;;false;">当他人表现出敌意时，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-4" style="width: 1586px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3910px;left: 6429px;z-index: 35;;;;;;false;">首先检查自己是否表现</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-19" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4158px;left: 1429px;z-index: 36;;;;;;false;">出了进攻的倾向。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4150px;left: 2700px;z-index: 37;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-17" style="width: 2536px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 1747px;z-index: 38;;;;;;false;">不要让怀疑为自己关上帮助的大门。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-4" style="width: 1110px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 4260px;z-index: 39;;;;;;false;">在感情关系中，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-4" style="width: 2538px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 5346px;z-index: 40;;;;;;false;">自己的怀疑破坏了双方信任的基础。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-0" style="width: 158px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 7859px;z-index: 41;;;;;;null;">他</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-3" style="width: 3806px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 1429px;z-index: 42;;;;;;false;">们真的值得信任吗？你总是在大脑中突出对方的弱点。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4645px;left: 5239px;z-index: 43;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-20" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4901px;left: 1747px;z-index: 44;;;;;;false;">不要总是与他人划清界限。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-20" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4901px;left: 3613px;z-index: 45;;;;;;false;">不要总是询问他人的立场。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-17" style="width: 2536px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4901px;left: 5479px;z-index: 46;;;;;;false;">注意到自己总是希望就指导方针与他</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-0" style="width: 950px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 1429px;z-index: 47;letter-spacing: 0.32px;;;;;;false;">人达成一致。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5141px;left: 2381px;z-index: 48;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-18" style="width: 4124px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5396px;left: 1747px;z-index: 49;;;;;;false;">打断自己对他人的观察，不要总是强调他人是否言行一致。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5388px;left: 5875px;z-index: 50;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-6" style="width: 3330px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5644px;left: 1747px;z-index: 51;;;;;;false;">注意到什么时候自己的思维取代了感觉和冲动。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5636px;left: 5081px;z-index: 52;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-4" style="width: 5870px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5892px;left: 1747px;z-index: 53;;;;;;false;">不要总是把别人看作是没有能力或者不值得信任的人，好像其他人都是行动的阻碍。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5884px;left: 7621px;z-index: 54;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-18" style="width: 4600px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6139px;left: 1747px;z-index: 55;;;;;;false;">学会保持联系。不要因为害怕而退出，并认为是对方抛弃了自己。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6131px;left: 6352px;z-index: 56;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-0" style="width: 5076px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6387px;left: 1747px;z-index: 57;letter-spacing: 0.53px;;;;;;false;">注意到自己喜欢怀疑他人的好意和恭维，尤其是在自己放松警惕的时候。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-21" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6387px;left: 6828px;z-index: 58;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-4" style="width: 1110px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6387px;left: 6897px;z-index: 59;;;;;;false;">在我毫无准备的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-19" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6635px;left: 1429px;z-index: 60;;;;;;false;">时候就会被击中。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-21" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6635px;left: 2698px;z-index: 61;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6626px;left: 2770px;z-index: 62;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-4" style="width: 3966px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6882px;left: 1747px;z-index: 63;;;;;;false;">承认自己胆量不够。总是需要得到权威的认可才敢行动。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6874px;left: 5715px;z-index: 64;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-3" style="width: 3806px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7130px;left: 1747px;z-index: 65;;;;;;false;">注意自己喜欢质疑权威，而不是去寻找双方的共同点。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7122px;left: 5557px;z-index: 66;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-14" style="width: 6348px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7378px;left: 1747px;z-index: 67;;;;;;false;">认识到自己往往只会想起糟糕的事情而不是快乐的经历。提醒自己去回忆那些快乐的记忆。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-9" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7626px;left: 1429px;z-index: 68;;;;;;null;">6</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-17" style="width: 3170px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 7626px;left: 1509px;z-index: 69;;;;;;false;">号性格者总是喜欢在负面记忆的轨道上行驶。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 7617px;left: 4683px;z-index: 70;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-11" style="width: 3344px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7873px;left: 1749px;z-index: 71;letter-spacing: 1.1500000000000001px;;;;;;false;">利用自己的想象力，去想象和表达正面的结果。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-0" style="width: 2852px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7873px;left: 5098px;z-index: 72;letter-spacing: 0.38px;;;;;;false;">如果记忆总是集中在糟糕的结果上，那就</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-22" style="width: 4758px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8121px;left: 1429px;z-index: 73;;;;;;false;">通过想象力把负面的结果夸大，让自己发现原来现实还不是最糟的。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8113px;left: 6192px;z-index: 74;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-9" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8368px;left: 1747px;z-index: 75;;;;;;null;">6</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-0" style="width: 632px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8368px;left: 1827px;z-index: 76;;;;;;false;">号性格者</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-11" style="width: 2868px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8368px;left: 2459px;z-index: 77;letter-spacing: 1.25px;;;;;;false;">需要一步一步脚踏实地地接近自己的目标</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-0" style="width: 2687px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 8368px;left: 5333px;z-index: 78;;;;;;false;">，而不是采取错误鲁莽的行为来掩饰内</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-19" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8616px;left: 1429px;z-index: 79;;;;;;false;">心的害怕。他们还</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-11" style="width: 3186px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8616px;left: 2698px;z-index: 80;letter-spacing: 1.21px;;;;;;false;">需要注意，不要让过去的负面经历影响了自己</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-0" style="width: 158px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8616px;left: 5889px;z-index: 81;;;;;;null;">。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8608px;left: 6045px;z-index: 82;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-15" style="width: 318px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8864px;left: 1429px;z-index: 83;;;;;;false;">六、</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-16" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8864px;left: 1749px;z-index: 84;;;;;;null;">6</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-11" style="width: 1749px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8864px;left: 1829px;z-index: 85;letter-spacing: 0.98px;;;;;;false;">号需要注意避免的做法：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8856px;left: 3580px;z-index: 86;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-13" style="width: 2854px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9111px;left: 1747px;z-index: 87;;;;;;false;">对潜在的帮助表示怀疑，宁愿自己单干。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9103px;left: 4605px;z-index: 88;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-17" style="width: 2536px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9359px;left: 1747px;z-index: 89;;;;;;false;">对成功感到害怕。害怕超越了父母。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9351px;left: 4287px;z-index: 90;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-0" style="width: 4563px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9607px;left: 1747px;z-index: 91;letter-spacing: -0.74px;;;;;;false;">随着畏惧感的产生，觉得自己变得被动了，觉得自己失去了棱角，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-0" style="width: 1725px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9607px;left: 6291px;z-index: 92;letter-spacing: -1.28px;;;;;;false;">开始犹豫不决，不愿再把</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-0" style="width: 792px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9855px;left: 1429px;z-index: 93;letter-spacing: 0.39px;;;;;;false;">项目完成。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9847px;left: 2223px;z-index: 94;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-10" style="width: 3012px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10102px;left: 1747px;z-index: 95;;;;;;false;">希望自己比那些准备帮助自己的人更出色。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10094px;left: 4763px;z-index: 96;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-22" style="width: 5711px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10350px;left: 1747px;z-index: 97;;;;;;false;">喋喋不休。让大脑控制了心灵。让言语和分析取代了实际行动和来自内心的感受。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10342px;left: 7463px;z-index: 98;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-6" style="width: 1744px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10598px;left: 1747px;z-index: 99;;;;;;false;">越来越明显的自我怀疑，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-4" style="width: 2538px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10598px;left: 3453px;z-index: 100;;;;;;false;">而且很容易把怀疑投影到他人身上，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-5" style="width: 2060px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10598px;left: 5955px;z-index: 101;;;;;;false;">认为是他人对自己的能力产生</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-0" style="width: 632px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10845px;left: 1429px;z-index: 102;;;;;;false;">了怀疑。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10837px;left: 2063px;z-index: 103;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-5" style="width: 792px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11093px;left: 1747px;z-index: 104;;;;;;false;">妄自尊大。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-4" style="width: 2062px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11093px;left: 2501px;z-index: 105;;;;;;false;">把改变的过程弄得过于复杂。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-19" style="width: 3488px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11093px;left: 4527px;z-index: 106;;;;;;false;">对结果不切实际的幻想阻碍了完成现实目标的逻辑</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-0" style="width: 474px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11341px;left: 1429px;z-index: 107;;;;;;false;">行动。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11332px;left: 1905px;z-index: 108;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s11-8" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 11584px;left: 1429px;z-index: 109;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p></div></div></div>

</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-22" style="width: 1584px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4553px;left: 1747px;z-index: 30;;;;;;false;">需要保持高度的兴奋。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-15" style="width: 1426px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4553px;left: 3282px;z-index: 31;;;;;;false;">同时参与多项活动，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-23" style="width: 1586px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4553px;left: 4659px;z-index: 32;;;;;;false;">对很多事情都感兴趣。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-24" style="width: 1904px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4553px;left: 6194px;z-index: 33;;;;;;false;">喜欢保持感情的高峰状态。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-5" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4544px;left: 8023px;z-index: 34;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-17" style="width: 4600px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4800px;left: 1747px;z-index: 35;;;;;;false;">保持多种选择，并把这当作一种避免对单一任务进行承诺的工具。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-5" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4792px;left: 6352px;z-index: 36;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-25" style="width: 4440px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5048px;left: 1747px;z-index: 37;;;;;;false;">用快乐的精神活动，比如谈话、计划和思考，取代深层的接触。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-5" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5040px;left: 6192px;z-index: 38;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-26" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5295px;left: 1747px;z-index: 39;;;;;;false;">避免与他人发生直接冲突。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-5" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5287px;left: 3652px;z-index: 40;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-22" style="width: 1584px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5543px;left: 1747px;z-index: 41;;;;;;false;">喜欢把信息相互关联，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-23" style="width: 1110px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5543px;left: 3308px;z-index: 42;;;;;;false;">进行系统分析，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-24" style="width: 1904px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5543px;left: 4394px;z-index: 43;;;;;;false;">这种注意力方式可以导致：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-18" style="width: 1744px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5543px;left: 6273px;z-index: 44;;;;;;false;">从有困难或有限制的任务</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-17" style="width: 5394px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5791px;left: 1429px;z-index: 45;;;;;;false;">中理智地逃脱；从不相关或者看似矛盾的观点中找到不寻常的联系和相似点。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-5" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5783px;left: 6826px;z-index: 46;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-9" style="width: 1108px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6038px;left: 1747px;z-index: 47;letter-spacing: 0.27px;;;;;;false;">在某种意义上，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-14" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6038px;left: 2856px;z-index: 48;;;;;;null;">7</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-27" style="width: 5076px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6038px;left: 2936px;z-index: 49;;;;;;false;">号并没有生活在真正的情感生活中，因为他们的内心总是充满了关于情感</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-28" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6286px;left: 1429px;z-index: 50;;;;;;false;">关系的各种想象。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-5" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6278px;left: 2700px;z-index: 51;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-10" style="width: 1273px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6534px;left: 1429px;z-index: 52;letter-spacing: 1.1700000000000002px;;;;;;false;">三、适合的环境：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-5" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6525px;left: 2703px;z-index: 53;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-20" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 6781px;left: 1749px;z-index: 54;;;;;;null;">7</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-10" style="width: 6188px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 6781px;left: 1829px;z-index: 55;letter-spacing: 0.56px;;;;;;false;">号性格者可以成为编辑、作家或者讲故事的人。他们往往是新模式的理论家。他们是计划</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-10" style="width: 4937px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7029px;left: 1429px;z-index: 56;letter-spacing: 1.1500000000000001px;;;;;;false;">者、组织者和创意收集者。他们寻找让自己情绪积极向上的自然途径。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-0 reader-word-s12-21" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7021px;left: 6371px;z-index: 57;font-size: 167px;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-23" style="width: 1586px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7277px;left: 1747px;z-index: 58;;;;;;false;">他们是永远的年轻人，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-23" style="width: 2062px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7277px;left: 3295px;z-index: 59;;;;;;false;">为了保持自身的健康和活力，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-16" style="width: 2696px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7277px;left: 5319px;z-index: 60;;;;;;false;">他们会经常光顾健身中心和保健食品商</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-9" style="width: 2995px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7525px;left: 1429px;z-index: 61;letter-spacing: -0.43999999999999995px;;;;;;false;">店。他们的形象会出现在医疗保健杂志上。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-9" style="width: 1428px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7525px;left: 4405px;z-index: 62;letter-spacing: 0.61px;;;;;;false;">他们是理想主义者、</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-9" style="width: 952px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7525px;left: 5814px;z-index: 63;letter-spacing: 0.65px;;;;;;false;">未来主义者，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-28" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7525px;left: 6748px;z-index: 64;;;;;;false;">也是世界级的旅行</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-9" style="width: 316px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7772px;left: 1429px;z-index: 65;;;;;;false;">者。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-29" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7772px;left: 1731px;z-index: 66;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-9" style="width: 3478px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7772px;left: 1802px;z-index: 67;;;;;;false;">我今天不能一直呆在这儿，我一会儿还要赶飞机。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-29" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7772px;left: 5268px;z-index: 68;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-9" style="width: 2681px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7772px;left: 5338px;z-index: 69;letter-spacing: -0.37px;;;;;;false;">他们总是会说。他们还是美食和美酒的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-17" style="width: 4124px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8020px;left: 1429px;z-index: 70;;;;;;false;">热衷者。在大学里，他们是跨学科研究的带头人和推动者。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-5" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8012px;left: 5557px;z-index: 71;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-13" style="width: 1433px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8267px;left: 1429px;z-index: 72;;;;;;false;">四、不适合的环境：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-5" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8259px;left: 2863px;z-index: 73;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-25" style="width: 2854px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8515px;left: 1747px;z-index: 74;;;;;;false;">通常，我们不会在例行公务的工作中看到</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-14" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8515px;left: 4603px;z-index: 75;;;;;;null;">7</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-18" style="width: 3330px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8515px;left: 4683px;z-index: 76;;;;;;false;">号的身影，因为这样的工作是没有冒险精神的。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-17" style="width: 4600px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8763px;left: 1429px;z-index: 77;;;;;;false;">实验室里的技术人员、会计和其他可以预计结果的工作，都不会是</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-14" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8763px;left: 6032px;z-index: 78;;;;;;null;">7</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-26" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8763px;left: 6112px;z-index: 79;;;;;;false;">号的选择。另外，他们也不</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-23" style="width: 2062px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9010px;left: 1429px;z-index: 80;;;;;;false;">喜欢为一个苛刻的老板工作。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-5" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9002px;left: 3492px;z-index: 81;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-19" style="width: 478px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9258px;left: 1429px;z-index: 82;;;;;;false;">五、对</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-20" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9258px;left: 1909px;z-index: 83;;;;;;null;">7</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-10" style="width: 1113px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9258px;left: 1987px;z-index: 84;letter-spacing: 1.09px;;;;;;false;">号有益的做法：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-5" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9250px;left: 3102px;z-index: 85;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-10" style="width: 5096px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9506px;left: 1749px;z-index: 86;letter-spacing: 1.11px;;;;;;false;">认识到自己总是被青春和活力所吸引。让自己看到年龄增长和成熟的价值</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-9" style="width: 158px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9506px;left: 6851px;z-index: 87;;;;;;null;">。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-5" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9498px;left: 7009px;z-index: 88;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-23" style="width: 1586px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9753px;left: 1747px;z-index: 89;;;;;;false;">学会让自己面对痛苦，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-23" style="width: 1110px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9753px;left: 3289px;z-index: 90;;;;;;false;">直到发现问题。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-9" style="width: 1111px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9753px;left: 4356px;z-index: 91;letter-spacing: 0.8200000000000001px;;;;;;false;">不要总是觉得：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-29" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9753px;left: 5428px;z-index: 92;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-28" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9753px;left: 5498px;z-index: 93;;;;;;false;">如果我需要帮助，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-9" style="width: 1270px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9753px;left: 6723px;z-index: 94;letter-spacing: 0.7000000000000001px;;;;;;false;">我就是有缺陷的。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-29" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9753px;left: 7951px;z-index: 95;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-5" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9745px;left: 8023px;z-index: 96;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-9" style="width: 6272px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10001px;left: 1747px;z-index: 97;letter-spacing: -1.25px;;;;;;false;">注意到自己出现精神逃避时的情况：过多计划、多项活动、新选择、未来设想。当自己的想</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-26" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10249px;left: 1429px;z-index: 98;;;;;;false;">法和活力都在高速运转时，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-14" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10249px;left: 3334px;z-index: 99;;;;;;null;">7</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-9" style="width: 1742px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10249px;left: 3414px;z-index: 100;letter-spacing: 0.32px;;;;;;false;">号实际上是在逃避现实。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-5" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10241px;left: 5159px;z-index: 101;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-25" style="width: 4440px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10497px;left: 1747px;z-index: 102;;;;;;false;">认识到自己喜欢去想象痛苦的感觉，而不是去接受真实的体验。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-5" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10489px;left: 6192px;z-index: 103;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-27" style="width: 5076px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10744px;left: 1747px;z-index: 104;;;;;;false;">注意到虚幻的快乐和缺乏深度的承诺会让人渴望得到更多的快乐和娱乐。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-5" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10736px;left: 6828px;z-index: 105;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-28" style="width: 3488px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10992px;left: 1747px;z-index: 106;;;;;;false;">不要沉迷于表面的快乐，而忽视了深层次的体验。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-5" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10984px;left: 5239px;z-index: 107;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-17" style="width: 4124px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11240px;left: 1747px;z-index: 108;;;;;;false;">不要用虚假或者不成熟的情感发泄取代深层次的情感反应。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-30" style="width: 2220px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11240px;left: 5797px;z-index: 109;;;;;;false;">注意到自己总是害怕做出深入的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-9" style="width: 474px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11487px;left: 1429px;z-index: 110;;;;;;false;">承诺。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-5" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11479px;left: 1905px;z-index: 111;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-16" style="width: 2696px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11735px;left: 1747px;z-index: 112;;;;;;false;">不要觉得自己总是应该获得特殊待遇。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-5" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11727px;left: 4447px;z-index: 113;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-30" style="width: 2220px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11983px;left: 1747px;z-index: 114;;;;;;false;">发现真正的责任范围，这往往比</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-14" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11983px;left: 3968px;z-index: 115;;;;;;null;">7</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-28" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11983px;left: 4048px;z-index: 116;;;;;;false;">号希望的要更大。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s12-5" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11974px;left: 5319px;z-index: 117;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p></div></div></div>

                <div class="ie-fix"><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-4" style="width: 3026px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1186px;left: 1749px;z-index: 2;letter-spacing: 1.18px;;;;;;false;">当内在的偏执情绪出现时，坚持脚踏实地。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-7 reader-word-s13-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 1178px;left: 4778px;z-index: 3;font-size: 167px;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-9" style="width: 2855px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1434px;left: 1747px;z-index: 4;;;;;;false;">发现他人的批评和自我评价之间的差异，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-10" style="width: 1586px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1434px;left: 4566px;z-index: 5;;;;;;false;">学会正确地评估自己。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-11" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1434px;left: 6114px;z-index: 6;;;;;;false;">注意到当自我价值遭到质疑</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-12" style="width: 4917px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1681px;left: 1429px;z-index: 7;;;;;;false;">时，自己会很害怕，会渴望重新振作起来，重新获得高人一等的感觉。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 1673px;left: 6350px;z-index: 8;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-15" style="width: 6345px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1929px;left: 1747px;z-index: 9;;;;;;false;">当良好的自我感觉遭到质疑时，尽管十分愤怒，也要学会控制自己的情绪，继续完成工作。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-16" style="width: 1426px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2177px;left: 1429px;z-index: 10;;;;;;false;">当情感出现问题时，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-17" style="width: 2222px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2177px;left: 2830px;z-index: 11;;;;;;false;">不要对爱人产生两极化的看法，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-12" style="width: 1744px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2177px;left: 5028px;z-index: 12;;;;;;false;">要么认为对方全是错的，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-18" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2177px;left: 6749px;z-index: 13;;;;;;false;">要么认为对方全是</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-19" style="width: 4758px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2424px;left: 1429px;z-index: 14;;;;;;false;">对的。如果事情看上去很糟糕，要学会接受现实，而不是胡思乱想。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2416px;left: 6192px;z-index: 15;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-9" style="width: 5552px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 1747px;z-index: 16;;;;;;false;">认识到自己喜欢把事物美化，喜欢让事情变得更有趣，总是想象得比实际更好。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2664px;left: 7305px;z-index: 17;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-19" style="width: 2696px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2920px;left: 1429px;z-index: 18;;;;;;false;">认识到自己喜欢为自己虚构一个故事，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-20" style="width: 1746px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2920px;left: 4087px;z-index: 19;;;;;;false;">以避免受到痛苦的伤害。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-15" style="width: 2220px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2920px;left: 5795px;z-index: 20;;;;;;false;">这种令人愉快的故事与事实关系</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-1" style="width: 632px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3167px;left: 1429px;z-index: 21;;;;;;false;">甚微，但</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-21" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3167px;left: 2061px;z-index: 22;;;;;;null;">7</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-10" style="width: 5870px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3167px;left: 2141px;z-index: 23;;;;;;false;">号会通过类推的办法把痛苦的情绪精神化，让注意力转移到精神画面上，从而阻止真</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-22" style="width: 1108px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3415px;left: 1429px;z-index: 24;;;;;;false;">正的痛苦体验。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3407px;left: 2539px;z-index: 25;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-11" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 1747px;z-index: 26;;;;;;false;">认识到自己喜欢逃避现实，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-15" style="width: 2220px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 3600px;z-index: 27;;;;;;false;">躲在自己的幻想和虚假情感中。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-1" style="width: 1428px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 5769px;z-index: 28;letter-spacing: 0.61px;;;;;;false;">学会生活在现实中，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-20" style="width: 952px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 7146px;z-index: 29;;;;;;false;">而不是逃避。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3654px;left: 8023px;z-index: 30;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-19" style="width: 4758px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3910px;left: 1747px;z-index: 31;;;;;;false;">舍弃没有实现的选择。不必因为失去选择而产生遭到现实的害怕感。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3902px;left: 6510px;z-index: 32;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-4" style="width: 318px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4158px;left: 1429px;z-index: 33;letter-spacing: 1.7999999999999998px;;;;;;false;">六、</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-5 reader-word-s13-8" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4158px;left: 1749px;z-index: 34;font-size: 158px;;;;;;null;">7</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-4" style="width: 1431px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4158px;left: 1829px;z-index: 35;letter-spacing: 1.02px;;;;;;false;">号需要避免的做法：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4150px;left: 3262px;z-index: 36;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-23" style="width: 1584px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 1747px;z-index: 37;;;;;;false;">对心理治疗感到厌倦，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-12" style="width: 1744px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 3308px;z-index: 38;;;;;;false;">开始向心理医生献殷勤，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-1" style="width: 794px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 5028px;z-index: 39;letter-spacing: 0.8200000000000001px;;;;;;false;">送小礼物，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-15" style="width: 2220px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 5797px;z-index: 40;;;;;;false;">让自己的注意力转移到有趣的精</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-16" style="width: 792px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 1429px;z-index: 41;;;;;;false;">神追求上。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4645px;left: 2223px;z-index: 42;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-19" style="width: 6187px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4901px;left: 1747px;z-index: 43;;;;;;false;">觉得自己高人一等。瞧不起温柔的心理医生，认为对方很可笑。瞧不起普通百姓的生活。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4893px;left: 7939px;z-index: 44;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-12" style="width: 5393px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 1747px;z-index: 45;;;;;;false;">在遇到困难情况时，会在脑海中联想很多其他情况，让眼前的困难失去威力。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5141px;left: 7145px;z-index: 46;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-10" style="width: 5870px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5396px;left: 1747px;z-index: 47;;;;;;false;">当承诺出现问题时，希望加速完成自己的活动。在失去其他选择时，感到焦虑不安。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5388px;left: 7621px;z-index: 48;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-18" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5644px;left: 1747px;z-index: 49;;;;;;false;">对承诺感到厌烦。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-24" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5644px;left: 3018px;z-index: 50;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-20" style="width: 1746px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5644px;left: 3086px;z-index: 51;;;;;;false;">我想要回我的其他选择。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-24" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5644px;left: 4833px;z-index: 52;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5636px;left: 4906px;z-index: 53;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-18" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5892px;left: 1747px;z-index: 54;;;;;;false;">在乎自己的地位。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-24" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5892px;left: 3018px;z-index: 55;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-1" style="width: 3650px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5892px;left: 3086px;z-index: 56;letter-spacing: 0.59px;;;;;;false;">我站在哪儿？我的位置在哪儿？其他人怎么看我的？</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-21" style="width: 39px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5892px;left: 6739px;z-index: 57;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-24" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5892px;left: 6819px;z-index: 58;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5884px;left: 6889px;z-index: 59;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-9" style="width: 5076px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6139px;left: 1747px;z-index: 60;;;;;;false;">不想当领导，也不想被领导。希望与权威平起平坐，避免受到他们命令。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6131px;left: 6828px;z-index: 61;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-12" style="width: 4917px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6387px;left: 1747px;z-index: 62;;;;;;false;">一旦现有问题出现了好转，就想要离开心理治疗。急于恢复健康状态。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6379px;left: 6668px;z-index: 63;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-19" style="width: 3172px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6635px;left: 1747px;z-index: 64;;;;;;false;">喜欢改变，喜欢把现有问题赋予更高的含义。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6626px;left: 4923px;z-index: 65;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-1" style="width: 2536px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6882px;left: 1747px;z-index: 66;letter-spacing: 0.42999999999999994px;;;;;;false;">对过去的负面经历产生错误的回忆。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6874px;left: 4287px;z-index: 67;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-22" style="width: 1108px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7130px;left: 1747px;z-index: 68;;;;;;false;">通过取笑问题，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-16" style="width: 1426px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7130px;left: 2806px;z-index: 69;;;;;;false;">来表达自己的愤怒。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-12" style="width: 1744px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7130px;left: 4183px;z-index: 70;;;;;;false;">认为遇到的问题很可笑。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-17" style="width: 2222px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7130px;left: 5876px;z-index: 71;;;;;;false;">认为他人的担忧都是微不足道、</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-16" style="width: 792px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7378px;left: 1429px;z-index: 72;;;;;;false;">令人发笑的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7370px;left: 2223px;z-index: 73;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 7621px;left: 1429px;z-index: 74;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-26" style="width: 668px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8094px;left: 1429px;z-index: 75;;;;;;false;">九型人格</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 83px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8094px;left: 2097px;z-index: 76;;;;;;null;">8</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-25" style="width: 1501px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8094px;left: 2179px;z-index: 77;letter-spacing: -0.8400000000000001px;;;;;;false;">号－－义将、老大型</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8094px;left: 3679px;z-index: 78;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 1242px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 8560px;left: 1429px;z-index: 79;letter-spacing: -0.32px;;;;;;false;">2008-07-20 10:47 </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-26" style="width: 668px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9033px;left: 1429px;z-index: 80;;;;;;false;">九型人格</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 83px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9033px;left: 2097px;z-index: 81;;;;;;null;">8</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-25" style="width: 1002px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9033px;left: 2179px;z-index: 82;letter-spacing: -0.6900000000000001px;;;;;;false;">号领导特质：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9033px;left: 3180px;z-index: 83;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 9503px;left: 1429px;z-index: 84;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 9503px;left: 1512px;z-index: 85;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 9503px;left: 1596px;z-index: 86;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 9503px;left: 1680px;z-index: 87;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 9503px;left: 1764px;z-index: 88;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-25" style="width: 6178px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 9503px;left: 1846px;z-index: 89;letter-spacing: -0.62px;;;;;;false;">特别爱当老大、讲话有中气、喜欢控制别人、比较容易冲动、好打斗、武断、豪气、</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-26" style="width: 1169px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9751px;left: 1429px;z-index: 90;;;;;;false;">好买单、喜做主</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9751px;left: 2597px;z-index: 91;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 83px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 10220px;left: 1429px;z-index: 92;;;;;;null;">8</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-25" style="width: 3336px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 10220px;left: 1512px;z-index: 93;letter-spacing: -0.8200000000000001px;;;;;;false;">号才力：有义气、什么东西都自已扛、不服输</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 10220px;left: 4847px;z-index: 94;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-4" style="width: 638px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10693px;left: 1429px;z-index: 95;letter-spacing: 1.79px;;;;;;false;">一、困境</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10685px;left: 2067px;z-index: 96;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-21" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10941px;left: 1429px;z-index: 97;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-21" style="width: 39px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10941px;left: 1509px;z-index: 98;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-1" style="width: 3964px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 10941px;left: 1589px;z-index: 99;letter-spacing: 0.47px;;;;;;false;">他们的童年充满了斗争，强者受到尊敬，弱者被人欺负。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 10932px;left: 5557px;z-index: 100;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-19" style="width: 3172px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11188px;left: 1747px;z-index: 101;;;;;;false;">他们因此学会了保护自己，让自己变成强者。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11180px;left: 4923px;z-index: 102;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-10" style="width: 3966px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11436px;left: 1747px;z-index: 103;;;;;;false;">他们是愤怒的公牛，却愿意为弱小者提供安全的保护伞。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11428px;left: 5715px;z-index: 104;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-19" style="width: 5235px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11683px;left: 1747px;z-index: 105;;;;;;false;">他们可以不择手段地追逐权力和地位，目的却是让自己成为正义的执行者。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11675px;left: 6987px;z-index: 106;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-23" style="width: 1584px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11931px;left: 1747px;z-index: 107;;;;;;false;">小时候害怕受人欺负的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-21" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11931px;left: 3332px;z-index: 108;;;;;;null;">8</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-17" style="width: 4445px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11931px;left: 3412px;z-index: 109;;;;;;false;">号学会了保护自己，他们对于他人的侵犯和恶意变得特别敏感。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s13-13" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11923px;left: 7859px;z-index: 110;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;">

</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-9" style="width: 4282px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1434px;left: 1747px;z-index: 6;;;;;;false;">控制个人的占有物和空间，控制那些可能影响自己生活的人。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 1425px;left: 6034px;z-index: 7;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-10" style="width: 3172px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1681px;left: 1747px;z-index: 8;;;;;;false;">具有进攻性，公开地、毫不控制地表达愤怒是</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-11" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1681px;left: 4921px;z-index: 9;;;;;;null;">8</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-12" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1681px;left: 5001px;z-index: 10;;;;;;false;">号性格者的一种典型反应。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 1673px;left: 6906px;z-index: 11;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-12" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1929px;left: 1747px;z-index: 12;;;;;;false;">关注正义，喜欢保护他人。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 1921px;left: 3652px;z-index: 13;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-10" style="width: 5235px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2177px;left: 1747px;z-index: 14;;;;;;false;">把打架和性爱当作与他人接触的方式。相信那些在正面冲突中不退缩的人。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2168px;left: 6987px;z-index: 15;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-13" style="width: 4917px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2424px;left: 1747px;z-index: 16;;;;;;false;">把过度看作克服厌倦的良药。夜生活、疯狂娱乐、彻夜狂欢、暴饮暴食</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-14" style="width: 316px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2424px;left: 6668px;z-index: 17;;;;;;false;">……</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2416px;left: 6987px;z-index: 18;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-12" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 1747px;z-index: 19;;;;;;false;">难以意识到自我的依赖性。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-15" style="width: 1426px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 3626px;z-index: 20;;;;;;false;">当别人爱上他们时，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-16" style="width: 2540px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 5028px;z-index: 21;;;;;;false;">他们会通过各种方式拒绝真实情感，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-3" style="width: 474px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 7543px;z-index: 22;;;;;;false;">比如离</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-13" style="width: 3330px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2920px;left: 1429px;z-index: 23;;;;;;false;">开、认为无聊或者暗自谴责自己对他人的误导。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2911px;left: 4763px;z-index: 24;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-14" style="width: 70px;height: 175px;line-height: 175px;top: 3162px;left: 1747px;z-index: 25;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-3" style="width: 1270px;height: 175px;line-height: 175px;top: 3162px;left: 1815px;z-index: 26;letter-spacing: 0.7000000000000001px;;;;;;false;">要么全有要么全无</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-14" style="width: 70px;height: 175px;line-height: 175px;top: 3162px;left: 3086px;z-index: 27;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-3" style="width: 2679px;height: 175px;line-height: 175px;top: 3162px;left: 3157px;z-index: 28;letter-spacing: -0.5px;;;;;;false;">的关注方式，常常把所有事物极端化。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-3" style="width: 1430px;height: 175px;line-height: 175px;top: 3162px;left: 5817px;z-index: 29;letter-spacing: 0.8599999999999999px;;;;;;false;">他人要么是强大的，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-15" style="width: 792px;height: 175px;line-height: 175px;top: 3162px;left: 7229px;z-index: 30;;;;;;false;">要么是弱小</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-3" style="width: 6587px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3415px;left: 1429px;z-index: 31;letter-spacing: -1.22px;;;;;;false;">的，要么是公平的，要么是不公平的，没有中间类型存在。这种注意力的关注方式会导致：无法</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-9" style="width: 2220px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 1429px;z-index: 32;;;;;;false;">意识到自身的弱点，为了支持让</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-11" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 3650px;z-index: 33;;;;;;null;">8</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-17" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 3730px;z-index: 34;;;;;;false;">号感到惟一安全的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-14" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 5001px;z-index: 35;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-18" style="width: 318px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 5070px;z-index: 36;;;;;;false;">合法</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-14" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 5388px;z-index: 37;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-19" style="width: 2538px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 5458px;z-index: 38;;;;;;false;">观点而自动否定其他观点；在帮助他</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-19" style="width: 2062px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3910px;left: 1429px;z-index: 39;;;;;;false;">人的过程中给予适当的力量。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3902px;left: 3492px;z-index: 40;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-20" style="width: 2854px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4158px;left: 1587px;z-index: 41;;;;;;false;">他们建立信任的方法是完全地展示自我，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-10" style="width: 2696px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4158px;left: 4405px;z-index: 42;;;;;;false;">尽可能多地消除相互之间的未知信息，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-16" style="width: 952px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4158px;left: 7064px;z-index: 43;;;;;;false;">这种做法往往</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-10" style="width: 5711px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 1429px;z-index: 44;;;;;;false;">会强迫他人的选择立场，或者让自己处于有争议的立场中，以便观察他人的反应。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4398px;left: 7145px;z-index: 45;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-21" style="width: 950px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 1747px;z-index: 46;;;;;;false;">寻求控制也是</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-11" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 2698px;z-index: 47;;;;;;null;">8</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-9" style="width: 2220px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 2778px;z-index: 48;;;;;;false;">号天性中渴望公正的一种表现。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-11" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 4999px;z-index: 49;;;;;;null;">8</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-12" style="width: 1902px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 5079px;z-index: 50;;;;;;false;">号最关注的是权力和控制。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4645px;left: 6985px;z-index: 51;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-11" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 4901px;left: 1747px;z-index: 52;;;;;;null;">8</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-22" style="width: 6188px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 4901px;left: 1827px;z-index: 53;;;;;;false;">号性格者尊重公平的斗争。他们鄙视那些避免冲突的人，尊敬那些面对冲突依然坚持自己</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-13" style="width: 3330px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 1429px;z-index: 54;;;;;;false;">观点的人，因为他们觉得自己也属于这样的人。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5141px;left: 4763px;z-index: 55;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-11" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 5396px;left: 1747px;z-index: 56;;;;;;null;">8</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-15" style="width: 2694px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 5396px;left: 1827px;z-index: 57;;;;;;false;">号性格者习惯遵循自己的感觉和冲动。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 5388px;left: 4525px;z-index: 58;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-11" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 5644px;left: 1747px;z-index: 59;;;;;;null;">8</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-3" style="width: 790px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 5644px;left: 1827px;z-index: 60;;;;;;false;">号是典型的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-14" style="width: 70px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 5644px;left: 2620px;z-index: 61;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-15" style="width: 792px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 5644px;left: 2690px;z-index: 62;;;;;;false;">困难领导者</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-14" style="width: 70px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 5644px;left: 3483px;z-index: 63;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-20" style="width: 4440px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 5644px;left: 3555px;z-index: 64;;;;;;false;">，越是面对困难障碍时，他们越是表现出对领导权的忠诚，越能</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-23" style="width: 1584px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5892px;left: 1429px;z-index: 65;;;;;;false;">脱颖而出，直面挑战。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5884px;left: 3016px;z-index: 66;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-1 reader-word-s14-18" style="width: 638px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6139px;left: 1429px;z-index: 67;font-weight: 600;;;;;;false;">三、适合</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-6" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6139px;left: 2067px;z-index: 68;;;;;;null;">8</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-1" style="width: 795px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6139px;left: 2147px;z-index: 69;letter-spacing: 1.23px;;;;;;false;">号的环境：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6131px;left: 2943px;z-index: 70;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-23" style="width: 1584px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6387px;left: 1747px;z-index: 71;;;;;;false;">保护者常常会是政客，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-16" style="width: 2540px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6387px;left: 3284px;z-index: 72;;;;;;false;">或者那些在幕后操纵一切的政治家。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-19" style="width: 2062px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6387px;left: 5776px;z-index: 73;;;;;;false;">他们信奉的是黑手党的哲学：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-14" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6387px;left: 7796px;z-index: 74;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-3" style="width: 158px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6387px;left: 7865px;z-index: 75;;;;;;null;">我</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-17" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6635px;left: 1429px;z-index: 76;;;;;;false;">的地盘，我的人。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-14" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6635px;left: 2698px;z-index: 77;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-22" style="width: 5236px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6635px;left: 2768px;z-index: 78;;;;;;false;">他们是地狱的天使，是工会的领导人，是那种置于死地而后生的人。他们意</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-15" style="width: 1426px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6882px;left: 1429px;z-index: 79;;;;;;false;">志坚定但心地温和。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-16" style="width: 1746px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6882px;left: 2830px;z-index: 80;;;;;;false;">他们是一手掌握控制权，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-9" style="width: 2220px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6882px;left: 4552px;z-index: 81;;;;;;false;">一手把持公平原则的企业领导。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-17" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6882px;left: 6749px;z-index: 82;;;;;;false;">他们是分户出售公</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-13" style="width: 3330px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7130px;left: 1429px;z-index: 83;;;;;;false;">寓的地产开发商，带头为无家可归者提供住房。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7122px;left: 4763px;z-index: 84;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-1" style="width: 796px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7378px;left: 1429px;z-index: 85;letter-spacing: 1.33px;;;;;;false;">四、不适合</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-6" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7378px;left: 2227px;z-index: 86;;;;;;null;">8</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-1" style="width: 794px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7378px;left: 2307px;z-index: 87;letter-spacing: 0.8200000000000001px;;;;;;false;">号的环境：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7370px;left: 3102px;z-index: 88;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-19" style="width: 3966px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7626px;left: 1747px;z-index: 89;;;;;;false;">我们在需要良好表现和严格遵守规则的工作中，很难发现</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-11" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7626px;left: 5715px;z-index: 90;;;;;;null;">8</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-3" style="width: 2218px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7626px;left: 5795px;z-index: 91;letter-spacing: 0.37px;;;;;;false;">号性格者的身影。他们不喜欢那</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-3" style="width: 6505px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7873px;left: 1429px;z-index: 92;letter-spacing: 0.53px;;;;;;false;">些容易被不可预知的力量所操控的环境。他们不相信那些需要依靠领导者的好心才能完成的工</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-9" style="width: 2220px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8121px;left: 1429px;z-index: 93;;;;;;false;">作，也不喜欢待遇不公的地方。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8113px;left: 3652px;z-index: 94;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-5" style="width: 478px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8368px;left: 1429px;z-index: 95;;;;;;false;">五、对</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-6" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8368px;left: 1909px;z-index: 96;;;;;;null;">8</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-1 reader-word-s14-24" style="width: 1113px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8368px;left: 1987px;z-index: 97;font-weight: 600;;;;;;false;">号有利的做法：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8360px;left: 3102px;z-index: 98;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-10" style="width: 5711px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8616px;left: 1747px;z-index: 99;;;;;;false;">注意到自己总是要求对一段关系予以明确定义。把斗争看作发展信任的一种方式。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8608px;left: 7463px;z-index: 100;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-10" style="width: 2696px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8864px;left: 1747px;z-index: 101;;;;;;false;">注意到自己在感情关系或心理治疗中，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-3" style="width: 1904px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8864px;left: 4418px;z-index: 102;letter-spacing: 0.59px;;;;;;false;">总是要求建立清楚的规则。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-19" style="width: 1586px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8864px;left: 6298px;z-index: 103;;;;;;false;">但是一旦建立了规则，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-3" style="width: 158px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8864px;left: 7859px;z-index: 104;;;;;;null;">又</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-3" style="width: 1108px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9111px;left: 1429px;z-index: 105;letter-spacing: 0.27px;;;;;;false;">渴望破坏规则。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9103px;left: 2539px;z-index: 106;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-10" style="width: 2696px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9359px;left: 1747px;z-index: 107;;;;;;false;">注意到自己总是喜欢在身边寻找对手。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-9" style="width: 2220px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9359px;left: 4392px;z-index: 108;;;;;;false;">喜欢把周围的人都划分成两派，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-15" style="width: 792px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9359px;left: 6563px;z-index: 109;;;;;;false;">不是朋友，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-15" style="width: 792px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9359px;left: 7306px;z-index: 110;;;;;;false;">就是敌人。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-19" style="width: 2062px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9607px;left: 1429px;z-index: 111;;;;;;false;">通过挑衅，让对方采取行动。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9598px;left: 3492px;z-index: 112;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-9" style="width: 3806px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9855px;left: 1747px;z-index: 113;;;;;;false;">认识到自己的厌烦感觉，实际上是在掩盖其他的情感。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9847px;left: 5557px;z-index: 114;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-3" style="width: 4600px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10102px;left: 1747px;z-index: 115;letter-spacing: 0.52px;;;;;;false;">努力发现他人行为的逻辑性和正确性，允许他人坚持不同的观点。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10094px;left: 6352px;z-index: 116;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-19" style="width: 3014px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10350px;left: 1747px;z-index: 117;;;;;;false;">认识到真正的感觉往往是从消沉中产生的。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-3" style="width: 2380px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10350px;left: 4723px;z-index: 118;letter-spacing: 0.5800000000000001px;;;;;;false;">把消沉当作一种感情流露的方式，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-21" style="width: 950px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10350px;left: 7065px;z-index: 119;;;;;;false;">不要逃避负面</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-3" style="width: 474px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10598px;left: 1429px;z-index: 120;;;;;;false;">情绪。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10590px;left: 1905px;z-index: 121;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-10" style="width: 5711px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10845px;left: 1747px;z-index: 122;;;;;;false;">注意到什么时候对物质的滥用。不要让对他人的控制欲，取代了自己的真实希望。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10837px;left: 7463px;z-index: 123;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-17" style="width: 3488px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11093px;left: 1429px;z-index: 124;;;;;;false;">注意到自己对公正的追求和渴望保护他人的想法，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-10" style="width: 3172px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11093px;left: 4845px;z-index: 125;;;;;;false;">常常把周围的人分成了朋友和敌人两大对立的</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-3" style="width: 474px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11341px;left: 1429px;z-index: 126;;;;;;false;">阵营。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11332px;left: 1905px;z-index: 127;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-17" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11588px;left: 1747px;z-index: 128;;;;;;false;">把自己的注意力从</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-14" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11588px;left: 3018px;z-index: 129;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-24" style="width: 635px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11588px;left: 3086px;z-index: 130;;;;;;false;">你的方式</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-11" style="width: 178px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11588px;left: 3763px;z-index: 131;letter-spacing: -0.67px;;;;;;false;">vs.</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-19" style="width: 634px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11588px;left: 3942px;z-index: 132;;;;;;false;">我的方式</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-14" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11588px;left: 4576px;z-index: 133;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-13" style="width: 3330px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11588px;left: 4649px;z-index: 134;;;;;;false;">上转移出来，尽量认识到各个观点之间的相互联</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-3" style="width: 316px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11836px;left: 1429px;z-index: 135;;;;;;false;">系。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s14-7" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11828px;left: 1747px;z-index: 136;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p></div></div></div>
