                <div class="ie-fix"><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-3" style="width: 2538px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1186px;left: 1747px;z-index: 2;;;;;;false;">记得把自己的想法和感受记录下来，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-0" style="width: 2065px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1186px;left: 4247px;z-index: 3;letter-spacing: 0.76px;;;;;;false;">和自己的强迫性健忘作斗争。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-5" style="width: 1744px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1186px;left: 6274px;z-index: 4;;;;;;false;">用自己记录下来的想法和</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-6" style="width: 2854px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1434px;left: 1429px;z-index: 5;;;;;;false;">感受提醒自己不要强迫拒绝内心的感觉。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 1425px;left: 4287px;z-index: 6;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-10" style="width: 3806px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1681px;left: 1747px;z-index: 7;;;;;;false;">学会延迟情感的表达。在准备发火之前，先在心里倒数</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-11" style="width: 159px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1681px;left: 5557px;z-index: 8;letter-spacing: 0.8999999999999999px;;;;;;false;">10</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-0" style="width: 316px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1681px;left: 5717px;z-index: 9;;;;;;false;">下。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 1673px;left: 6034px;z-index: 10;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-12" style="width: 4124px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 1929px;left: 1747px;z-index: 11;;;;;;false;">不要总是从外界寻找问题的根源，学会从自己身上找问题。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 1921px;left: 5875px;z-index: 12;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-0" style="width: 1584px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2177px;left: 1747px;z-index: 13;letter-spacing: 0.36px;;;;;;false;">学会承认自己的错误。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2168px;left: 3334px;z-index: 14;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-14" style="width: 318px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2424px;left: 1429px;z-index: 15;letter-spacing: 1.7999999999999998px;;;;;;false;">六、</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-13 reader-word-s15-17" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2424px;left: 1749px;z-index: 16;font-size: 158px;;;;;;null;">8</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-14" style="width: 1431px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2424px;left: 1829px;z-index: 17;letter-spacing: 1.02px;;;;;;false;">号需要避免的做法：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2416px;left: 3262px;z-index: 18;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-0" style="width: 2536px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 1747px;z-index: 19;letter-spacing: 0.42999999999999994px;;;;;;false;">把他人的帮助误认为对自己的怜悯。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2664px;left: 4287px;z-index: 20;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-5" style="width: 3330px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2920px;left: 1747px;z-index: 21;;;;;;false;">喜欢控制细节。在行动中对一些小事要求苛刻。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-18" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2920px;left: 5081px;z-index: 22;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-0" style="width: 2856px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2920px;left: 5150px;z-index: 23;letter-spacing: 0.5800000000000001px;;;;;;false;">除非我找到我最喜欢的那把汤勺，不然宴</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-0" style="width: 950px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3167px;left: 1429px;z-index: 24;letter-spacing: 0.32px;;;;;;false;">会到此为止。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-18" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3167px;left: 2379px;z-index: 25;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3159px;left: 2451px;z-index: 26;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-19" style="width: 6187px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3415px;left: 1747px;z-index: 27;;;;;;false;">把潜在的帮助拒之门外。对他人的优点只字不提。行事鲁莽，把人得罪了自己还不知道。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3407px;left: 7939px;z-index: 28;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-0" style="width: 6272px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 1747px;z-index: 29;letter-spacing: -1.24px;;;;;;false;">忘记自己的目标。沉浸于过度的狂欢、食物、性爱、毒品之中。觉得越多就是越好。吃着碗</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-0" style="width: 1426px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3910px;left: 1429px;z-index: 30;letter-spacing: 0.41000000000000003px;;;;;;false;">里的，望着锅里的。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3902px;left: 2858px;z-index: 31;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-10" style="width: 2220px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4158px;left: 1747px;z-index: 32;;;;;;false;">对自己看不顺眼的人发出攻击。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4150px;left: 3970px;z-index: 33;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-10" style="width: 3806px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 1747px;z-index: 34;;;;;;false;">难以妥协。要么控制，要么离开。不会看到中间立场。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4398px;left: 5557px;z-index: 35;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-10" style="width: 4282px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 1747px;z-index: 36;;;;;;false;">不想让自己表现出依赖性。把他人的疏忽看作对诚信的背叛。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4645px;left: 6034px;z-index: 37;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-12" style="width: 4124px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4901px;left: 1747px;z-index: 38;;;;;;false;">关闭自己的感觉。有时候会放弃所有事物，什么也不关心。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4893px;left: 5875px;z-index: 39;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-3" style="width: 3966px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 1747px;z-index: 40;;;;;;false;">为了掩藏自身的弱点，而谴责他人，从他人身上挑毛病。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5141px;left: 5715px;z-index: 41;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-19" style="width: 2696px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5396px;left: 1747px;z-index: 42;;;;;;false;">制定规则，并把规则强加于他人身上。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5388px;left: 4447px;z-index: 43;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-10" style="width: 4282px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5644px;left: 1747px;z-index: 44;;;;;;false;">破坏自己的规则，说明自己是权力的掌控者，是不受约束的。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5636px;left: 6034px;z-index: 45;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-10" style="width: 2220px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5892px;left: 1747px;z-index: 46;;;;;;false;">失败以后陷入绝望，不能自拔。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s15-8" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5884px;left: 3970px;z-index: 47;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;">

</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-10" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2424px;left: 1747px;z-index: 21;;;;;;false;">关注他人的立场。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-15" style="width: 1428px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2424px;left: 2990px;z-index: 22;;;;;;false;">这种注意力会导致：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-16" style="width: 1586px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2424px;left: 4394px;z-index: 23;;;;;;false;">难以保持个人的立场，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-16" style="width: 2062px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2424px;left: 5955px;z-index: 24;;;;;;false;">但是却能拥有感知他人内心体</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-17" style="width: 950px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 1429px;z-index: 25;;;;;;false;">验的能力。与</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-18" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 2379px;z-index: 26;;;;;;null;">2</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-16" style="width: 634px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 2459px;z-index: 27;;;;;;false;">号性格者</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-13" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 3096px;z-index: 28;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-19" style="width: 476px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 3164px;z-index: 29;;;;;;false;">给予者</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-13" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 3641px;z-index: 30;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-16" style="width: 1110px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 2672px;left: 3711px;z-index: 31;;;;;;false;">有相似的地方。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 2664px;left: 4824px;z-index: 32;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-18" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 2920px;left: 1747px;z-index: 33;;;;;;null;">9</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-14" style="width: 6186px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 2920px;left: 1827px;z-index: 34;;;;;;false;">号性格者习惯把自身的能量和注意力从真正的需要中挪开，他们常常表现出怠惰的特征。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 180px;line-height: 180px;top: 2911px;left: 8017px;z-index: 35;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-18" style="width: 79px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 3167px;left: 1747px;z-index: 36;;;;;;null;">9</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-3" style="width: 6192px;height: 170px;line-height: 170px;top: 3167px;left: 1827px;z-index: 37;letter-spacing: 0.64px;;;;;;false;">号往往能够让两性关系维持很久，即便是在最初的甜蜜感已经荡然无存后，他们也会习惯</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-20" style="width: 4440px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3415px;left: 1429px;z-index: 38;;;;;;false;">性地保持这段关系，哪怕这种关系已经不再是他们的真实选择。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3407px;left: 5874px;z-index: 39;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-1" style="width: 638px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 1429px;z-index: 40;letter-spacing: 1.79px;;;;;;false;">三、适合</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-21" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 2067px;z-index: 41;;;;;;null;">9</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-22" style="width: 795px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3662px;left: 2147px;z-index: 42;;;;;;false;">号的环境：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 3654px;left: 2943px;z-index: 43;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-3" style="width: 158px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3910px;left: 1747px;z-index: 44;;;;;;null;">对</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-18" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3910px;left: 1905px;z-index: 45;;;;;;null;">9</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-3" style="width: 6034px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 3910px;left: 1985px;z-index: 46;letter-spacing: 0.66px;;;;;;false;">号有吸引力的环境是那些有条不紊的环境，每天的工作都根据日程安排、协议以及公认</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-14" style="width: 5711px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4158px;left: 1429px;z-index: 47;;;;;;false;">的程序在进行。他们适合做办公室的工作，以及那些需要对细节进行关注的工作。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4150px;left: 7145px;z-index: 48;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-22" style="width: 795px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 1429px;z-index: 49;;;;;;false;">四、不适合</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-21" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 2227px;z-index: 50;;;;;;null;">9</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-1 reader-word-s16-19" style="width: 794px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4406px;left: 2307px;z-index: 51;font-weight: 600;;;;;;false;">号的环境：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4398px;left: 3102px;z-index: 52;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-16" style="width: 634px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 1747px;z-index: 53;;;;;;false;">很少会有</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-18" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 2381px;z-index: 54;;;;;;null;">9</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-3" style="width: 5558px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4653px;left: 2461px;z-index: 55;letter-spacing: 0.67px;;;;;;false;">号性格者去做那些需要光鲜形象、不断自我推销的工作。他们也不喜欢那种工作</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-3" style="width: 5713px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4901px;left: 1429px;z-index: 56;letter-spacing: 0.5700000000000001px;;;;;;false;">程序会随时变化的工作。那些一味强调理论，而不注重细节和结构的工作，也不受</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-18" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4901px;left: 7145px;z-index: 57;;;;;;null;">9</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-3" style="width: 790px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 4901px;left: 7225px;z-index: 58;;;;;;false;">号的青睐。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 4893px;left: 8017px;z-index: 59;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-23" style="width: 478px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 1429px;z-index: 60;;;;;;false;">五、对</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-21" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 1909px;z-index: 61;;;;;;null;">9</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-1" style="width: 1113px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5149px;left: 1987px;z-index: 62;letter-spacing: 1.09px;;;;;;false;">号有益的做法：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5141px;left: 3102px;z-index: 63;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-14" style="width: 4758px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5396px;left: 1747px;z-index: 64;;;;;;false;">注意到自己总是想办法获得他人的积极评价，借此找到自己的位置。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5388px;left: 6510px;z-index: 65;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-3" style="width: 3012px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5644px;left: 1747px;z-index: 66;letter-spacing: 0.44999999999999996px;;;;;;false;">注意到自己喜欢把他人变成决定的参照物：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-13" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5644px;left: 4763px;z-index: 67;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-3" style="width: 1904px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5644px;left: 4833px;z-index: 68;letter-spacing: 0.59px;;;;;;false;">我是同意他，还是反对他？</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-13" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5644px;left: 6739px;z-index: 69;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5636px;left: 6811px;z-index: 70;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-24" style="width: 3806px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 5892px;left: 1747px;z-index: 71;;;;;;false;">不要让举棋不定的困惑取代了自己的真实感觉和愿望。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 5884px;left: 5557px;z-index: 72;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-20" style="width: 4440px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6139px;left: 1747px;z-index: 73;;;;;;false;">让工作项目有计划地进行，设定最后期限来帮助自己集中精力。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6131px;left: 6192px;z-index: 74;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-25" style="width: 2536px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6387px;left: 1747px;z-index: 75;;;;;;false;">不要保留自己的意见，把它说出来。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6379px;left: 4287px;z-index: 76;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-10" style="width: 3488px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6635px;left: 1747px;z-index: 77;;;;;;false;">学会一心一意地完成任务，不要被其他事情分心。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6626px;left: 5239px;z-index: 78;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-24" style="width: 6345px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 6882px;left: 1747px;z-index: 79;;;;;;false;">不要把注意力转移到不必要的替代品上，比如食品或电视。要及时注意到这种情绪的出现。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 6874px;left: 8023px;z-index: 80;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-24" style="width: 2220px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7130px;left: 1762px;z-index: 81;;;;;;false;">不要向他人去寻求决定的答案。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-18" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7130px;left: 3980px;z-index: 82;;;;;;null;">9</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-3" style="width: 3958px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7130px;left: 4060px;z-index: 83;letter-spacing: 0.21000000000000002px;;;;;;false;">号很清楚自己不想要什么，但是却不知道自己要什么，不</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-10" style="width: 2378px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7378px;left: 1762px;z-index: 84;;;;;;false;">过他们可以通过排除法找到答案。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7370px;left: 4144px;z-index: 85;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-24" style="width: 4282px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7626px;left: 1747px;z-index: 86;;;;;;false;">要练习既能从他人的立场上行动，又能从自己的立场上行动。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7617px;left: 6034px;z-index: 87;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-26" style="width: 3648px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 7873px;left: 1747px;z-index: 88;;;;;;false;">在注意力分散到不必要的事物上时，学会限制自己。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 7865px;left: 5399px;z-index: 89;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-3" style="width: 5552px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8121px;left: 1747px;z-index: 90;letter-spacing: 0.53px;;;;;;false;">关注眼前的下一步，而不是最终的目标，因为最终的目标需要一步一步地实现。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8113px;left: 7305px;z-index: 91;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-14" style="width: 2696px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8368px;left: 1747px;z-index: 92;;;;;;false;">注意到自己面对压力时，会变得顽固。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8360px;left: 4447px;z-index: 93;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-24" style="width: 2220px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8616px;left: 1747px;z-index: 94;;;;;;false;">通过想像力来释放自己的愤怒。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-15" style="width: 2698px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8616px;left: 3929px;z-index: 95;;;;;;false;">想像自己说出或做出了最糟糕的事情，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-27" style="width: 1426px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8616px;left: 6589px;z-index: 96;;;;;;false;">直到内心的怒火得到</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-3" style="width: 474px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 8864px;left: 1429px;z-index: 97;;;;;;false;">消减。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 8856px;left: 1905px;z-index: 98;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-23" style="width: 318px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9111px;left: 1429px;z-index: 99;;;;;;false;">六、</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-21" style="width: 79px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9111px;left: 1749px;z-index: 100;;;;;;null;">9</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-1" style="width: 1431px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9111px;left: 1829px;z-index: 101;letter-spacing: 1.02px;;;;;;false;">号需要避免的做法：</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9103px;left: 3262px;z-index: 102;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-25" style="width: 2536px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9359px;left: 1747px;z-index: 103;;;;;;false;">依赖他人的帮助，不愿与他人分开。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9351px;left: 4287px;z-index: 104;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-20" style="width: 4440px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9607px;left: 1747px;z-index: 105;;;;;;false;">责备他人。因为过于在意他人的愿望，一旦出现问题，就会产生</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-13" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9607px;left: 6192px;z-index: 106;;;;;;null;">“</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-17" style="width: 950px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9607px;left: 6263px;z-index: 107;;;;;;false;">都是他们的错</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-13" style="width: 70px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9607px;left: 7213px;z-index: 108;;;;;;null;">”</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-16" style="width: 634px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9607px;left: 7286px;z-index: 109;;;;;;false;">的想法。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 9598px;left: 7922px;z-index: 110;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-3" style="width: 5020px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9855px;left: 1747px;z-index: 111;letter-spacing: -1.19px;;;;;;false;">变得顽固。感到来自他人的压力。不愿把问题拿到桌面上来。僵持不动，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-10" style="width: 1268px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 9855px;left: 6748px;z-index: 112;;;;;;false;">逼着对方首先采取</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-3" style="width: 474px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10102px;left: 1429px;z-index: 113;;;;;;false;">行动。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10094px;left: 1905px;z-index: 114;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-25" style="width: 2536px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10350px;left: 1747px;z-index: 115;;;;;;false;">急需找到消磨时间和能量的新办法。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10342px;left: 4287px;z-index: 116;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-26" style="width: 4124px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10598px;left: 1747px;z-index: 117;;;;;;false;">恍惚。在谈话的时候注意力不集中，同时想着好几件事情。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10590px;left: 5875px;z-index: 118;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-24" style="width: 3806px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 10845px;left: 1747px;z-index: 119;;;;;;false;">无法注意到真正的需要，让琐事占据了自己的注意力。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 10837px;left: 5557px;z-index: 120;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-25" style="width: 2536px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11093px;left: 1747px;z-index: 121;;;;;;false;">习惯按部就班，从事机械性的动作。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11085px;left: 4287px;z-index: 122;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-16" style="width: 5870px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11341px;left: 1747px;z-index: 123;;;;;;false;">麻木、无动于衷。期望事情自己结束，而不是主动表明态度。不希望听到负面信息。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11332px;left: 7621px;z-index: 124;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> </p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-14" style="width: 3172px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11588px;left: 1747px;z-index: 125;;;;;;false;">总是需要得到更多的信息，等待他人的解释。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-11" style="width: 41px;height: 167px;line-height: 167px;top: 11580px;left: 4923px;z-index: 126;;;;;;font-family: simsun;;"> 
</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-27" style="width: 1426px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11836px;left: 1747px;z-index: 127;;;;;;false;">工作无法善始善终。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-3" style="width: 1270px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11836px;left: 3148px;z-index: 128;letter-spacing: 0.7000000000000001px;;;;;;false;">感觉受到了骚扰，</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-15" style="width: 1428px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11836px;left: 4394px;z-index: 129;;;;;;false;">不想认真对待工作。</p><p class="reader-word-layer reader-word-s16-24" style="width: 2220px;height: 158px;line-height: 158px;top: 11836px;left: 5797px;z-index: 130;;;;;;false;">希望用最小的投入换得最大的收
</p></div></div></div>
